Transportation After the Takeover of the North China War Zone 66

=Japanese Troops Refuse to Return Tianjin-Taierzhuang Communications Cables=

=Japanese Troops Still Occupy Luanyu Section to Transport Grain to Rehe=

=Travelers Between Tangshan and Luanyu Repeatedly Searched by Japanese Troops=

Beiping correspondence: Liu Shirun, a member of the War Zone Receiving Committee, recently went to Tianjin to negotiate with the Japanese garrison regarding traffic in eastern Luan and the return of buildings occupied by the Japanese army. He returned to Beiping yesterday afternoon. According to Liu, "Since the start of the Sino-Japanese War, Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao were the first to be impacted. When Shimenzhai and Haiyangzhen were tense, the Tianjin garrison headquarters and the Qinhuangdao garrison used telegrams to report news at any time. There are three types of Chinese telegraph lines between Tianjin and Qinhuangdao: (1) ordinary long-distance lines, (2) telegraph lines, and (3) special lines for the Beining Railway. The Beiping authorities inquired about the front-line situation at any time, and the Japanese army stationed in Qinhuangdao also used these three types of lines at will. When our army withdrew from Ludong, the Beining Railway only went to Tanggu, and the three types of telegraph lines between Tianjin and Qinhuangdao became the property of the Japanese. Now that the Tanggu Agreement has been signed and we are taking back the lost territories, everything is generally completed, but the Japanese army still uses our telegraph lines to transmit news and has not returned them. We feel very inconvenient that the lost territories have been taken back, but the telephone and telegraph lines between Tianjin and Qinhuangdao have not been recovered. Moreover, foreign nationals in Beidaihe need to use the phone to transmit messages at any time, and they often complain about this. In order to reorganize the postal and telegraphic affairs after taking back the lost territories, the Ministry of Communications recently sent a technician to Beiping to discuss the matter and request the Japanese side to return the lines in accordance with the agreement in order to reorganize them, restore them to their original state, and facilitate transportation. I went to Tianjin from Beiping a few days ago to negotiate with the Japanese garrison in charge. According to the Boxer Protocol, the Japanese army is stationed along the Beining Railway, but there are no dedicated telephone lines along the line, and news from various places must be reported at any time. After negotiations, the Japanese army agreed to return all the occupied lines. After continued discussion, two long-distance round-trip lines dedicated to the Beining Railway were temporarily borrowed by the Japanese side. Both sides sent an engineer to start inspecting and repairing the lines, and one of the Beining Railway phone lines was selected to be repaired quickly for use. All telegrams must pass through the Luan River Railway Bridge. When He Jun (Zhu Guo) retreated during the war, the bridge was bombed and the telegraph lines were broken, and the line poles were tilted. Later, wooden poles were temporarily used to suspend the lines. We are now preparing to repair the telegraph lines here to avoid future failures. Also, after our army retreated along the railway line, the Japanese army followed up and occupied many houses along the line. During this negotiation, the Japanese army withdrew from Shanhaiguan. The garrison had occupied the staff quarters of the Tangshan Beining Railway Engineering Office and part of the Luan County Telegraph Bureau, which had not yet been returned. During this negotiation, the Japanese side agreed to return them, but the withdrawal and takeover of the Japanese army and the puppet government agencies in Lin Yu County are still not completed, and negotiations have not yet begun. Luan Dong and the area along the Great Wall have always been a den of bandits. After the war, they have become increasingly rampant. After taking over the lost territories in Luan Dong and northern Beiping, we sent police, but their strength is weak, and the bandits are rampant and unscrupulous. According to statistics from various counties, the number of bandits is close to 200,000. However, according to investigations, although the bandits in various counties are rampant, they do not have the ability to unite. The people suffer unspeakable harm. In the future, suppressing them will require further negotiations with the Japanese side to formulate a comprehensive and concrete plan and send troops to carry out strict suppression in order to fundamentally solve the problem. However, the number of bandits is large and widespread. How to solve this problem and whether to find a way to make them surrender will depend on Chairman Yu (Xuezhong) after he arrives in Ji. There will be a solution. I will go to Tianjin again in three to five days."

Furthermore, according to Yin Tong, a member of the War Zone Receiving Committee, "The Japanese army in Luandong plans to transport military grain from Shanhaiguan to Rehe before the river freezes in winter. They are borrowing the railway from Shanhaiguan to Luanxian and leaving a small number of troops along the railway to protect the military transportation. We have contacted the Japanese side several times regarding the troop stationing issue and the Japanese army's use of vehicles hindering our traffic. It has now been decided that the Japanese army will only transport one train of grain per day until Hebei freezes. The freight will be temporarily recorded, and the Japanese troops along the route will also withdraw at that time. The reorganization of the puppet army in Yu Tian County has not yet been completed. It is still commanded by Hu Xie Wu. Dong Tianhua, the former county magistrate of that county, was beaten and insulted by the soldiers of that unit and left the county to report to the provincial government in Tianjin. The unit has now dismissed Zhang Qingxin, the officer in charge, and more than twenty soldiers responsible for the incident and expelled them. Hu Xie Wu and the local chamber of commerce have repeatedly telegraphed County Magistrate Dong to urge him to return to his post. Wei Jian, the director of the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government, summoned Dong yesterday for instructions. Dong is scheduled to return to Yutian today (31st) to resume his post. Regarding the suppression of bandits in Luandong, due to the ceasefire agreement, our army is not allowed to directly send troops into Luandong to suppress bandits, and the security force is weak, resulting in rampant bandits. This matter can be resolved after Chairman Huang and Chairman Yu return to the north."

Yesterday, someone from Shanhaiguan talked about what he saw along the way after the opening of the Ping-Yu section of the Beining Railway. He said, "Shanhaiguan is the junction of the Ping-Yu section and the puppet Anfeng Railway. Passengers from both sides change trains here. Passengers getting off the puppet railway and planning to take the Ping-Yu train west must get off here. Japanese military police and puppet police inspect and search Chinese passengers one by one. The situation is extremely serious. Japanese and Korean passengers are allowed to pass without being searched. Passengers getting off the Ping-Yu train to take the puppet Anfeng train are checked even more strictly. After boarding the Ping-Yu train, at stations such as Qinhuangdao, Beidaihe, Luanxian, and Tangshan, only Japanese military police change shifts and escort the train. However, at all stations along the way, Japanese military police board the train and patrol. If they encounter anyone resembling a soldier, they will interrogate them. After arriving at Lutai, our cavalry is stationed at the station and only boards the train to inspect. The interrogation situation is more relaxed than that of the Japanese military police. East of Tangshan, Japanese peddlers who specialize in selling prohibited items such as Jin Dan and morphine, as well as Japanese prostitutes, are extremely prevalent. All sovereignty is still in the hands of the Japanese. The so-called Ping-Yu through train is no different from traveling on borrowed land. The guest also said that in the Luandong area, because our sovereignty has not been fully recovered, bandits are rampant and causing disturbances, especially in the Qinhuangdao and Beidaihe areas. It is said that there are about 20,000 bandits, led by the bandit leader 'Old Mouse'. The Beining Railway Security Team is currently concentrated between Qinhuangdao and Beidaihe to protect the route. When the train arrives at the Qinhuangdao and Beidaihe stations, the security team stationed there will board the locomotive for protection. In the other carriages, there are more than three security team members protecting the train. The seriousness of the situation is enough to make passengers tremble. However, the order on the coast of Beidaihe is still stable. There are still more than a dozen Westerners staying there for summer vacation. The security there is the responsibility of Li Baozhen, the vice president of the Gongli Society. The president is still concurrently the director of the Beining Railway Bureau." (September 1st)

Suiyuan Also Reports Flooding 67

=Many Canals in Various Counties Are Destroyed=

=The Situation Is Serious and There Is No Hope for the Autumn Harvest=

Suiyuan Correspondence: Suiyuan in recent years can truly be said to have had natural disasters and man-made disasters one after another. The great drought of the 17th and 18th years of the Republic left the countryside in ruins after the famine. Selling wives and children was extremely tragic for a time. Last year, there was a gradual turnaround, but the low price of millet hurt farmers, and it turned into a strange phenomenon of "harvesting into disaster". This year, due to continuous rain and torrential mountain floods, the counties along the river have become flooded again, with submerged fields, collapsed houses, and the deaths of people and livestock, which is quite serious. The worst are Baotou, Salaqi County, and Tuoketuo County. There are also signs of disaster in the Hetao and Wulin areas. There is no hope for the autumn harvest, and relief is urgently needed. The arrival of Sun Dianying's army and the gathering of large troops have also created supply difficulties. The formation of this flood was caused by the destruction of many canals in various counties. For example, the Salaqi-Tuoketuo Minsheng Canal has not been released since the gate was opened. This project was severely damaged, with losses in the hundreds of thousands of yuan. The Yihe Canal in Zhungeer Banner in Tuoketuo County was breached, the canal body was completely destroyed, and the Minli Canal in Tuoketuo County was also affected. The breach of the cart dam has widened the flooded area. It has always emphasized water conservancy, but today it has been harmed by water, which was also unexpected. The formation of the flood in Salaqi County was originally due to torrential mountain floods, which were blocked by the Minsheng Canal. The water was blocked by the canal back that stretched from east to west and had nowhere to be discharged, so the villages on the north bank were submerged. Later, the north bank of the Minsheng Canal was destroyed, and the water flowed south, and the south bank was also destroyed, and the disaster area became larger. All the way to Tuoketuo County, water puddles hundreds of miles long and thirty, twenty, ten, or eight miles wide are everywhere, and they are all vast and have become Ze country. The west of the county seat of Tuoketuo County is close to the Heihe River. Decades ago, there were often Guan Polan, so the river embankment was repaired every year and was extremely strong. The willows lined up on the embankment are all decades of growth. In the past twenty years, the small river near the city has almost dried up, and even the Yellow River has been cut off. Therefore, building embankments is no longer necessary, and the trees on the embankment were cut down a few years ago. The trees were sold by the local government and government offices, and the roots were dug up by the poor to burn as firewood. Although new trees have been embellished every year in recent years, unfortunately, none have survived. Therefore, the river embankment was destroyed, and the river bank was loose. This year, the river water suddenly rose, and the people were caught off guard. A few days ago, a drama was performed in the River God Temple for three days, but it was still impossible to celebrate Anlan forever. The county government urged the people to build embankments and guarded them day and night. Residents living near the river tore down houses to block the water, and finally the county seat was able to survive, but the disaster in the villages west of the river was extremely severe. In recent days, Baotou, Salaqi County, and Tuoketuo County have been rushing to the provincial government to ask for relief. The situation is summarized as follows:

Baotou 68

The fourth district of Baotou suffered the most severe disaster. On August 16th and 17th, the water came like a tide, breaking through the walls from Dongda Shetubao and entering the area like a mountain falling. The people were unable to prevent it, causing the houses in the fort to be submerged. Because it was daytime, the people were awakened and ran to the northwest corner of the high mound to take temporary refuge. After the water receded, the people in the fort were homeless. Thousands of people were starving and sleeping in the open, and the situation was extremely tragic. Regarding the losses, this one fort was flooded with more than 70 houses, more than 3,000 stones of grain, and hundreds of cattle, horses, pigs, and sheep. The crops outside the fort were silted up by the sand. More than 3,000 farmers, men, women, old and young, are now sleeping on the beach without clothes or food, crying from hunger and cold day and night. The Baotou County Government has telegraphed the provincial government to request emergency relief. The climate in Suiyuan Province is cold, and it has been very cold in recent days. It is feared that people will freeze and starve.

Salaqi County 69

The disaster in Salaqi County is the most serious. The county seat is almost a Ze country. There are more than a hundred villages surrounded by water. Mountain water has erupted everywhere, and the Yellow River flows north. The area is the widest. What was usually land in the past must now be traveled by boat. In villages with walled castles, the lives of the people can still be protected. In villages without walled castles, it is unimaginable if the rescue is not timely. In the most urgent time, in Dadaicun Village, more than a thousand villagers were using all their strength to seize the dam every day. There are many places where boats are traveling near the Sui-Bao Railway, such as Daxiaoeergexuncun, Gongjiban, and Taosihai.

Tuoketuo County 70

The villages west of the county seat of Tuoketuo County are completely submerged. County Magistrate Chen Yingdao recently reported to the provincial government, saying, "The river floods have risen sharply and flooded the area. The eight villages in Hexi Station area in the first district and the villages of Nanyaozi and Liangjianfang in the second district were submerged one after another. The number of people and livestock drowning in the water is countless. Those who have barely escaped have no place to eat during the day and no place to sleep at night. They are carrying their children and dragging their daughters, dragging mud and water, and crying from hunger and cold. It is unbearable to hear." This is the truth. He asked the provincial government for emergency relief. The provincial government is facing many difficulties.

Chiang Orders Xu Yuanquan, Et Al., to Be Responsible for Capturing and Executing Bandit Leaders 71

=He Long's Bandits in Western Hubei Occupy Songzi=

=Local Bandits in Eastern Hubei Disturb Huangma=

Hankou Correspondence: He Long's remaining bandits in western Hubei suddenly set off from near Yuyangguan on the 25th of last month and captured Songzi County. County Magistrate Jiang Wenbo was killed. The bandits also have the potential to invade Jingzhou and Shashi. Songzi County is located on the south bank of the Yangtze River. It was originally called Mopanshi and moved here not long ago. It faces Shashi and Jiangling across the river. Because there are no heavy troops stationed there, the local defense force is also very weak. This was detected by the bandits, who took advantage of the opportunity to invade. County Magistrate Jiang led the local defense force to fight back, but they were defeated due to being outnumbered. Jiang was brutally killed by the bandits, and many people were also harmed. After capturing Songzi, the bandits tried to cross the river and take advantage of the victory. There were about two or three thousand bandits. Xu Yuanquan had just returned to Shashi from Hankou and immediately sent a large army to suppress them in several directions after receiving the report. The bandits could not withstand the pressure and retreated in panic. It is reported that Songzi City has now been recovered and the remaining bandits are being searched for. The provincial government received a telegram from Xu one day, saying that the county magistrate of Songzi County was brutally killed by the bandits and that no one was in charge of the county. The people were shaken and hoped that the provincial government would send a cadre to come quickly to stabilize the situation and reassure the people. The provincial government discussed the matter and decided to appoint Wang Wanjia, the county secretary of the county, to act as the agent temporarily and telegraphed Xu to inform him.

In the Huangma area of eastern Hubei, bandits have now invaded again. It seems that they are the main force of the bandits. Liu Zhenhua has ordered Sun Lianzhong, Wan Yaohuang, and Peng Zhenshan to jointly suppress them and has reported to Commander-in-Chief Chiang to transfer Li Yutang's Third Division stationed in northern Henan to assist. They will disembark in Xiaogan and march on foot towards Huangma. Chiang telegraphed Xu Yuanquan, Liu Zhenhua, and Chen Jicheng on the 2nd, assigning Xu to capture and execute He Long, the bandit leader in western Hubei; Chen to capture and execute Zhang Tao and Ye Jinbo, the bandit leaders in southern Hubei; and Liu to capture and execute Shen Zemin, Lu Huanxian, and Liao Rongkun, the bandit leaders in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, in order to eliminate the major criminals and eliminate the bandit scourge. If the bandit leaders are not captured, even if the bandits are cleared, it will not be considered a complete task. (September 2nd)

Zhang Qun Goes to Hunan to Meet He Jian 72

=To Discuss the Aftermath of the Bandit Area in Southern Hubei and Investigate Hunan Politics=

=The Provincial Government Organizes a Provincial County Government Inspection Team=

Hankou Correspondence: Zhang Qun, chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, believes that the political affairs facilities in Hunan and Hubei are closely related. At the beginning of his appointment, he planned to go to Hunan to discuss everything with He Jian, chairman of Hunan. Later, when Zhang went to Lushan to meet Chiang Kai-shek, he received a telegram from He, saying that the aftermath of the bandit area in southern Hubei urgently needed to be discussed in person. He had originally planned to come to Hubei for advice, but he was unable to do so due to a slight illness. He especially requested Zhang to visit Hunan. Zhang replied that he would agree. Recently, the National Society of Engineers held its third annual meeting in Wuchang. Hu Shuhua, director of the Hunan Construction Department, came to Hubei to attend the meeting and was ordered by He to visit Zhang and urge him to go. Zhang and Li Fanyi, director of the Construction Department, and Cheng Qibao, director of the Education Department, took a special train on the Hunan-Hubei Railway south at 5:00 p.m. on the 1st. Feng Fei, secretary of the provincial government, accompanied him. It is said that the mission of this trip, in addition to discussing the aftermath of the bandit area in southern Hubei, also includes discussing water conservancy issues, such as dredging rivers and lakes, and requesting the central government to approve the plans. They will also inspect the administrative, construction, education, Qingxiang, and Baojia facilities in Hunan Province, as well as the rural conditions, for Hubei Province to learn from. It is planned to stay in Hunan for five days and then return to Hubei. During the period of going to Hunan, all provincial government affairs will be handled by Lu Zhu, the commissioner and secretary-general. The Hubei provincial government has been planning the aftermath of the bandit area and has decided to allocate 100,000 yuan to southern Hubei, eastern Hubei, and western Hubei. The headquarters has approved the record. The county government inspection in each county has also been decided. The provincial government, the four departments of civil affairs, finance, construction, and education, and the security department will each send five people to form the "Hubei Provincial County Government Inspection Team." The province will be divided into five inspection areas: east, west, south, north, and central. The team will depart in groups, first going to the three areas of eastern Hubei, western Hubei, and southern Hubei, where banditry is more rampant, and then to the two areas of northern Hubei and central Hubei. The scope of the inspection includes: (1) civil affairs facilities, (2) financial revenue and expenditure, (3) construction progress, (4) education situation, (5) training of security teams, (6) general situation of Baojia household registration, and (7) local customs and people's hardships, etc. It is planned to formulate various plans based on the inspection reports to be the goal of implementing new policies. This work can be completed in one and a half months. (September 1st)

Record of a Trip to Shandong 73

Because the reporter participated in the 10th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society, I traveled by sea to Qingdao. After the meeting, I toured Jinan and Tai'an, then took the Jinpu and Jinghu railway lines back to Shanghai. What I heard and saw on this trip is worth recounting, so I will record one or two aspects below:

Mr. Liang Shuming has dedicated himself to the rural construction movement in Shandong in recent years, and is well-known to the world. The Economic Society invited him to speak at the meeting, and his topic was "The Special Difficulties in Solving China's Economic Problems." His main idea was that China only has two economic paths forward: 1) The government effectively maintains order and security in all regions, and the economy is left to free competition and free development by the people; 2) In addition to maintaining order and security, the government further develops industries and implements a controlled economy. Although both paths are viable, considering China's current situation, foreign economic forces have already deeply penetrated the interior. If the government can only maintain security and order, the result of free competition in the economy will be that foreign economic forces will increasingly dominate, and China's nascent agricultural and industrial sectors will be overwhelmed by foreign forces and cannot avoid the misfortune of bankruptcy. Therefore, if we take the first path, the future is very dangerous. As for the second path, it is naturally more in line with China's current situation, but it requires the government to be healthier, more powerful, and more transparent to even discuss it. Otherwise, it is no different from quenching thirst by looking at plums. Today's political conditions in China are truly inadequate. We cannot even achieve the first path, let alone take a further step to implement a controlled economy. From this, it is clear that seeking an economic way out today faces special difficulties. The crux of these difficulties lies in the unresolved political problems. Therefore, those who discuss economic problems and study economic plans today must pay attention to political problems. Moreover, the occurrence of economic problems each has its special social circumstances as a background. Therefore, in discussing economic plans, in addition to paying attention to political problems, one must also deeply understand the individuality of all aspects of society. Only in this way can all economic plans be relevant and effective. Otherwise, even with plans, they will be nothing more than castles in the air.

After the speech, Mr. Liang had a private conversation with the reporter. He said, "What troubles China the most now is that whether individuals, groups, local or central authorities, all are bound and oppressed by the environment, eking out a living in contradictions, so that all strength is mostly consumed in useless places. If this situation does not change, the vitality of each person cannot be fully developed." Furthermore, he said, "The progress of society and the evolution of the country depend on the development of each person's life force. Now that our people cannot fully develop their inherent life force, it is a major reason why all undertakings are not easy to progress." Also, "China's society is a rural economic society, so all construction undertakings and economic plans must start from the rural aspect. The solution to China's problems lies in the solution to rural problems." This is a view that Mr. Liang firmly believes in. When discussing rural issues, the rural economic situation in Shandong Province can serve as a valuable reference. I will now provide a brief report to the readers:

Peanuts are an important agricultural product in Shandong Province. In the past, if a farming family had ten or eight mu of land to plant peanuts, they could live comfortably for a year. These peanuts were shipped to the United States to make peanut oil and sold everywhere. Now, due to the world economic panic and the decline of all industries, peanut sales are also greatly sluggish, and prices are half of what they used to be. Therefore, all farming families who plant peanuts are in danger of bankruptcy. This is a major blow to the rural economy in Shandong Province. Wheat is also an important agricultural product in Shandong Province. Now that the US wheat loan has been completed, there is also a fear of wheat sales being sluggish in Shandong. It is said that for this reason, the farmers are mostly worried.

Japanese merchants in various parts of China recently elected representatives two weeks ago to hold a commercial joint meeting in Qingdao. The purpose was to promote the sales of Japanese goods in China. It is said that one of the resolutions was "We must find ways to make Chinese transportation agencies abolish differential treatment for Chinese and Japanese goods." Many Japanese goods, such as matches, are in a competitive position with those made in our country. Because they have sufficient capital and better technology, the cost of these goods is low, and they already have an advantage in sales. If this resolution of the Japanese is achieved, it will be easier to dump their goods, and goods made in our country will be more affected. Yesterday, a friend talked about this, saying that Japan and the Northeast puppet state under Japanese influence are almost using their entire strength to deal with self-made products in China. However, industries in North China each act on their own and rarely have a spirit of unity and cooperation, let alone concentrate their efforts to compete with foreign countries. Therefore, the commercial crisis in North China is actually no less than the agricultural economic crisis. Qingdao is a good ice-free port in Shandong, and although there is much room for future development, the Japanese are ambitious and are using this as a center for dumping Japanese goods in various parts of North China. As a reporter traveling through this place, I cannot help but feel anxious.

丨Fees are levied on people, animals, and goods丨

Inspection Report of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei Provinces 75

Special correspondent of this newspaper, Ren An

A General View of the Collapse of Agriculture in Jiangxi Province

Nanchang special dispatch: Our country is established on agriculture, and the total number of farmers accounts for more than 78% of the total population of the country, and the national economy is also completely based on the rural economy. However, in recent years, due to the deep invasion of international capitalism from the outside, and the alternating cycle of natural and man-made disasters from the inside, the rural economy has tended to collapse fundamentally. As a result, the great waves that have arisen and will arise in society all take this as the main force for turbulence. This is probably because farmers have established their extremely important position in society in terms of their large numbers and production relations. The reporter inspected Jiangxi Province for half a month, passed through more than 20 counties, and conducted rural surveys in half of them. Now, I will briefly describe the general situation of production in Jiangxi Province, as follows:

According to the report of the "Domestic Rural Improvement Project Inspection Team" of the province, the total area of cultivated land in the province is about 40 million mu, and there are about 3 million farming households. Each farming household can obtain an average of 13 mu. The annual output of major crops is more than 84 million dan of rice, timber is worth about 8 million yuan, tea is more than 200,000 boxes. In addition, cotton, peppermint, camphor, tea oil, beans, etc., because there are no detailed surveys and statistics, the exact figures are not yet known. Handicrafts such as porcelain, the annual output is worth about 10 million yuan, summer cloth is about 5 million yuan, paper is about 8 million yuan, and mineral products such as tungsten in various counties in southern Jiangxi, coal in Pingxiang Yugan and other counties, and iron in Yongxin Jiujiang and other counties, occupy an important position in the production of the province. The output of tungsten accounts for 80% of the national output and half of the world's output. Since the 16th year of the Republic of China, production has gradually declined. In the 20th year, the province's exports were only worth 17 million taels, while the imports in the same year were as high as 41 million taels. Last year's summer cloth production was only about 30% of the usual level, and tea losses were estimated at more than 1 million yuan. Compared with the 16th year of the Republic of China, porcelain production decreased by more than 4 million yuan, and the production and sales of paper have plummeted. During the flood two years ago, a large amount of Saigon rice was shipped from Shanghai, and the supply of flour was entirely imported. With the drastic reduction in productivity and the sudden increase in the number of unemployed people, the strong risk and the weak turn to the ditches. Among the counties in the province, only more than 20 counties such as Nanchang and Xinjian are free from bandits. In addition, more than 50 counties have suffered from banditry. Those who have suffered the most have been left with barren fields and villages in ruins. This is enough to see the general collapse of the countryside.

Furthermore, an analysis of the individual status of the tranquil areas, the semi-bandit areas, and the bandit areas: 1) Tranquil areas: on the surface, it seems that people can live and work in peace and contentment, but in essence, due to the great impact of the so-called scissors-shaped price of selling agricultural products at low prices and purchasing industrial products at high prices, as a result, various agricultural and industrial products in the past five years have not been able to make ends meet, the burden has become heavier, and the losses have increased. One has to sell his land. Therefore, most farmers have become tenant farmers, and tenant farmers have become hired laborers. Under the opposing development of capitalism and pre-capital, pre-capital will inevitably decline, that is, the small-scale peasant economy will inevitably collapse, and the situation of increasing land concentration and increasing poverty of small farmers will be formed. However, the small farmers suffer greatly from the low prices of agricultural products, but the landlords do not make much progress. In addition, the taxes and duties are heavy, and both landlords and tenants feel the pain of being unable to compensate for their losses. Occasionally, there are those who flee to other places and leave their fields barren. 2) Semi-bandit areas: First, due to the social instability and the low prices of agricultural products, the rich are afraid of chaos and fly away. Although farmers and small and medium-sized landlords want to avoid chaos, they have no way to sell their land and have to stick to their homeland. Large landlords and hired laborers are more mobile, that is, they can easily flee to other places. The percentage of self-cultivating farmers seems to have increased relatively. Moreover, because no one buys land, the land is not concentrated. The landlords cannot take care of the land. In order to have some income rather than nothing, they have to improve the conditions of tenancy and try to rent out the land. The small and medium-sized self-cultivating farmers are also very willing to cultivate this land with better conditions in order to make up for the loss of the collapse of their side business. However, in the end, the big problems of "cultivation may not yield a harvest" and "harvest may not be sold at a good price" linger in their minds. They often reduce fertilizer and labor, and maintain the mentality of letting the land produce on its own. As a result, the output decreases sharply, fertile land becomes barren land, and small pieces of wasteland gradually increase. At the same time, rural finance flows out invisibly to stable commercial areas, and even if farmers want to borrow at high interest rates, no one dares to lend money. 3) Bandit areas: The degree of destruction in the areas of military and bandit wars is truly a wilderness. If it is a guerrilla zone, that is, a place where the main forces of the army and bandits do not directly confront each other, there are small groups of bandits that come and go from time to time. Ignorant farmers are often attracted. It is uncertain whether the land is cultivated. Only life and property are extremely dangerous.

The Jiangxi Provincial Government organized a domestic rural improvement project inspection team. In November last year, it sent Wang Zhenxin and others to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, Hebei and other provinces to inspect the rural improvement project. It took several months before they returned to Jiangxi. Recently, Wang initiated the organization of the Jiangxi Rural Improvement Society in order to contact comrades and implement improvement measures to the countryside. I recently visited Wang, and we talked for a long time about his feelings about the inspection of rural improvement projects in various places and the Jiangxi rural improvement plan. According to the talk, I (Wang's self-proclaimed) led the inspection team to various provinces to inspect the rural improvement projects, and I believe that the rural projects in various places seem to have their special characteristics. Among them, there are many projects that focus on education as the center, and there are also those that simultaneously carry out various aspects of politics and economy. However, due to different subjective opinions, some only focus on Eastern culture and ignore the background of the times, and some only pay attention to domestic factors and forget the economic aggression of foreign countries. However, on the whole, they can fully express their enthusiasm and spirit of sacrifice for rural projects. This is the best impression I have gained. The Jiangxi countryside is already on the verge of complete collapse. After I came back from the inspection, I had some ideas on the rural improvement in our province, namely: 1) The situation of the collapse of the Jiangxi countryside is different from that in other places, and the rescue methods cannot be completely imitated from other places. 2) Rural improvement should focus on the rural economy, and rural organizations, rural education, etc. should also advance simultaneously. In other words, in order to pull the farmers back from the bandit areas and prevent the counties that have not been affected by banditry from being infected, we must give the farmers practical benefits, help them to be self-reliant, and establish the foundation of the rural economy. Then all other undertakings can be carried out smoothly, and the means to achieve the improvement of the rural economy is to use political power to develop the economy, and then popularize education and promote politics through economic development. Therefore, it is currently planned to first conduct various experimental work in the experimental areas of rural improvement, and then universally promote the results.

Songjiang 76

The Results of the Election of County Executive and Supervisory Committees Are Announced

The term of office of the executive and supervisory members of this county has expired. The county representative conference was opened on September 1st. The election was very fierce before the event, and rumors were rampant. However, the representative conference was held safely yesterday (1st). Zhang Bingyuan, Wu Guofang, and Jiang Zhishang were the presidium of the conference. The meeting opened at 9 am. Chairman Zhang Bingyuan reported, Commissioner Jin Tigian, Battalion Commander Jiang Yunqing of the Second Battalion of the Third Security Regiment, and Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Jing delivered speeches, and the provincial party headquarters instructor gave a speech. The conference continued in the afternoon. Gu Junjie, Xu Zhongming, and Yang Tianyi were appointed as the proposal review committee of the conference, and Yang Yunwen, Jia Xiang, and Yang Wenjun were appointed as the declaration drafting committee. The meeting opened this morning (2nd). Under the supervision of the provincial instructor, Wang Zhe Wu Jiaju, Sun Shiheng, Li Chang, and Xu Zhao were elected as executive members, and Shen Fuyun, Lu Shulian, and Tan Maireen were elected as supervisory members. Wu Guofang, Yao Qi, Lu Zhidao, and Jia Xiang were alternate executive and supervisory members. The representative conference continued in the afternoon. The county government's public security and education bureaus reported on the progress made in the past year as technical directors, etc. The third day of the representative conference was the 3rd, which was dedicated to discussing the proposals.

Wuxi 77

The Typhoon and Rain Affect the Crops

For nearly half a month in the county, thunderstorms have fallen from time to time, and the phenomenon of severe drought has changed to good weather. The crops are developing rapidly. If there are no special changes, there will be a very good harvest this winter, and the farmers are extremely happy. Unexpectedly, a hurricane suddenly rose the day before yesterday, passing through the county. Yesterday morning (3rd), the wind was even stronger and heavy rain fell. The ditches were full and the climate was gloomy and cold. It is said that if the hurricane and rain do not stop, the future of the crops will be affected.

Stopping the Opening and Relocation of New Cocoon Exchanges 78

This autumn cocoon market is scheduled to open scales today (4th). There are a total of ten cocoon markets that have reported to open in the past few days. Yesterday, eighteen more, including Lu Hengyi, Ruichangsheng, Shunchang, Hexing, and Yongda, reported to open. Including the previous ones, there are a total of twenty-eight. It is expected that there will be a large number of reports to open today or tomorrow. The county government of this county received instructions from the provincial government yesterday, roughly stating that the cocoon market in this province has been open with no restrictions in principle since the 18th year of the Republic of China. The "Provisional Cocoon Market Regulations of Jiangsu Province" were promulgated, allowing each county to establish cocoon markets. The number of cocoon markets is almost twice as many as before the opening, and the output of autumn cocoons has also increased year by year. However, because the local species are gradually being eliminated, the output of spring cocoons has not increased. The cocoon markets in various counties are inevitably oversupplied. Also, the silk industry in this province has adopted new machines to improve various silk-making technologies. Therefore, the former Department of Agriculture and Mines had already advocated the elimination of old cocoon markets and promoted the establishment of new-style cocoon drying machines to fundamentally improve the silk industry. Now, in order to adapt to the needs of the environment, the original provisional cocoon regulations should be revised. However, the opening of this year's autumn cocoon market is approaching, and there is not enough time for revision. Before the revision, all requests to open new and relocate cocoon markets will be temporarily suspended to avoid disputes. After Strict County Chief received the order, he has now complied with it.

Gaoyou 79

The Culpable Police Officer is Escorted to Guazhou for Interrogation

Yu Guosheng, a patrol officer of the Second Squad of the 23rd Team of the Provincial Public Security Force on the water stationed in 20Lipu, and patrol leader Li Deming, beat Haihai Newspaper interviewer Li Wei and Zhang Zhen's mother, Shi, and destroyed the town chief's residence. After Wang Baojing, the inspector of the Sixth District Department, investigated and reported the case, he received a secret order. At about 2 am yesterday (31st), Li led 40 box gun teams, disarmed the patrol officer Yu Guosheng, patrol leader Li Deming, and patrolman Yang Er at the Drug Investigation Office in Nanyuan Township, District 2, and escorted them to the Guazhou Sixth District Department for interrogation. On the afternoon of the same day, Squad Leader Deng, stationed in Lujin, sent a team to 20Lipu to bring back the remaining soldiers and ammunition to Lujin to prevent further incidents.

Two Villages in District Nine Suffered Bandit Looting 80

Beiwang and Xiqian villages in the ninth district of the county were suddenly attacked by 20 to 30 bandits at 12 am the day before yesterday. They were armed with box guns and rifles, spoke with a Cang-Fu accent, and poured into the villages to search every household without exception. The two villages were robbed of a lot of silver dollars, clothing and jewelry, and more than 400 shi of rice was stolen, and five civilian boats were taken away. It is reported that the losses were huge.

Jiashan 81

Typhoons Wreaked Havoc Over the Past Two Days

This county has suffered from insect plagues, and the people are unable to make a living. Last year, they were also affected by the low price of grain. Therefore, the farmers in the countryside all hope that this year's autumn harvest will be slightly better, so that they can survive. Unexpectedly, there have been typhoons and heavy rains day and night over the past two days. At this time, the drought-resistant rice is forming ears, and it has suffered a great loss due to the typhoon. Although the late rice sown by the migrants has all turned into grain, it has been blown down by the wind. Because of the accumulated water in the fields, it has all sprouted. The general farmers are all crying out in pain when they see this disaster. As for the collapse of houses and the overturning of boats, it is even more difficult to estimate.

Hangzhou

The Prosecutor Appeals Again in the Tao Jinzi Case 82

After the Supreme Court sent the case of Tao Jinzi, a female student of the West Lake Art School, who brutally killed her classmate Liu Ying, back to the Zhejiang Provincial High Court for retrial, Tao Jinzi was sentenced to life imprisonment and Xu Gewen was acquitted. Subsequently, Tao and Xu were summoned for a communist case, and Xu was detained in a military prison. The prosecutor filed a public prosecution against Tao and Xu for allegedly endangering the Republic of China. It is learned that Tao Jinzi's side stated that the ten-day period after the delivery of the judgment has expired, and Tao herself and her family members do not intend to appeal. However, prosecutor Ji Gengyang believed that Tao Jinzi had premeditated murder by turning off the lights and hiding them in her coat pocket, and asking the maid Chen Zhu to go out to buy Snow White Cream and lock the door. Xu Qinwen, as a man, allowed Liu Mengying, a girl under the age of 20, to stay overnight, which clearly showed an intention to commit adultery, which constituted a crime against the family. Yesterday (2nd), he specially appealed to the Supreme Court in accordance with the law.

The Hangzhou Municipal Party Committee Members Are Elected 83

The Hangzhou municipal party affairs were previously handled concurrently by the Hangzhou County Party Committee. In March, the provincial party committee decided to divide and establish a preparatory office. The first representative conference was held the day before yesterday, and the executive and supervisory members were elected at 2 pm yesterday (2nd). As a result, Xu Shiheng, Tong Mengsheng, Chen Wen, Wu Zhidao and other fourteen people were elected as executive members, and Zhu Huiqing, Yu Xuechen, Wan Deyi and other eight people were elected as supervisory members. After the provincial party committee approves them, they can be officially established.

A Middle School Teacher Commits Suicide by Taking Poison 84

Jin Yuchun, a physiology and hygiene teacher at Huilan Middle School in Shipalou, Hangzhou, is 33 years old, from Jinjiazhan, Zhuji. His family is well-off. His father is dead, and his mother is alive. His wife, Feng, has three sons, the eldest and youngest are at home. The second son, named Jin Zhu, was brought to Hangzhou by his father and is studying in the affiliated elementary school of the school. Jin is quite loyal, but he is short and is often ridiculed by others when he goes out. Therefore, Jin thought he was humiliated and had the idea of committing suicide last winter. Because he was detected early, he was able to be treated. Unexpectedly, after the school started on the 1st of this month, Jin also worked as usual, but his attitude was suddenly different. He often said to people, "Hangzhou people are paying attention to me, even rickshaw drivers are looking at me," and so on. Yesterday (3rd) at 8 am, Wang Yinian, the accounting director of the school, became suspicious because he had not seen Jin eating breakfast. He went to the bedroom to look and saw Jin lying down with his clothes on, his face was gray. He knew that he had taken poison. He hurriedly asked the school doctor Wang Jimin to come to the school for treatment. Because he had taken too much poison, he had already died. Principal Xu Yue, in addition to reporting the case to the court, also sent someone to Zhuji to inform the family members to come to Hangzhou to take care of the matter.

A Night Boat from Hangzhou to Huzhou is Robbed by Bandits 85

The night boat from Huzhou to Hangzhou was sailing downstream of Leidian at two o'clock last night when it suddenly saw two small boats with double oars flying forward, approaching the front of the boat, and shouting to stop the boat. Six bandits with guns swarmed on board. One bandit monitored the actions of the crew members, while the other bandits searched for silver notes and shouted away after they were finished. After checking the losses, the total was about 200 yuan. A loss list has been issued and submitted to the water police team for investigation.

Bengbu

Unemployed Youth Scams for Money 86

Shi Juefei, a youth from Zhengyangguan, Northern Anhui, was born into poverty and received secondary education. He has lived in Bengbu for several years. Last year, he was introduced by someone to work as a teacher at the Third Yiwu Elementary School in Fengyang County, Shou Changli, in this port. He falsely claimed that Zhou Dezhi, the director of the Provincial Third Mass Education Hall, Peng Zhuoru, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Xueluan, the public relations director of the Datong Coal Mine Company, were short of funds for the Third Yiwu Elementary School and solicited donations outside, and privately engraved Peng's and others' private seals and forged letters of introduction to solicit donations from all parties. The donations were all pocketed. The school authorities discovered this and immediately dismissed Shi's teaching position, and Shi became unemployed. Recently, due to the pressure of life, he relapsed and impersonated a staff member of the Third Mass Education Hall, carrying donation books and forged letters of introduction, and solicited donations from various institutions and groups. Yesterday, he solicited donations from the Stamp Tax Bureau of the 13th District of Hua Chang Street, and the bureau suspected that his behavior was suspicious. He immediately summoned the police to guard him and sent someone to the Mass Education Hall to ask if there was an employee Shi Mou soliciting donations outside. The hall denied it, and the police took Shi to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau for a brief interrogation, and then transferred him to the main bureau for county law enforcement.

Local News

Typhoon Passes Through, Baoshan Seawall in Danger Yesterday Afternoon 87

Xuejiatan Gulongdun Collapses in Ten Places

Only One or Two Feet Remain in Laoshidong and Other Places

Baoshan County Government Has Hired Civilian Labor to Rescue

County Chief Jin Wired the Provincial Authorities for Help Yesterday

Dabaishe reported that the typhoon passed through Taiwan on the evening of the 1st of this month. For days, the wind was strong and the rain was heavy, and the tide was fiercely pounding. For two consecutive days, it roared endlessly. The seawall in Baoshan County shields the counties of Shanghai, Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan, where the essence of the southeast is concentrated. It is extremely important. However, due to years of disrepair, it has been severely damaged. After the great flood in eighteen provinces two years ago, gentlemen from Shanghai and Baoshan and other places appealed, but due to limited funds, only selective repairs could be made. Since the day before yesterday, the rain and wind have been exceptionally violent, and the tide has been surging. By noon yesterday (3rd), the seawall had been washed away in many places, and the tide rushed in wildly, causing severe damage. Yesterday, the Baoshan county chief hired civilian labor to rescue and wired the provincial authorities for help. A reporter from Dabaishe heard the news and rushed to investigate. The details are recorded as follows:

Typhoon Passes Through 88

The typhoon blew into Baoshan County from the northeast on the evening of the 1st of this month, accompanied by heavy rain. By the evening of the 2nd, the situation was even worse, and the tide was fiercely pounding. The seawall in all places was in extremely dangerous condition, and the most dangerous places were only one or two feet high. Many of the long-distance telephone poles and wires installed throughout the county were broken by the wind. The cotton in the fields was flowering and fruiting, and almost all of it was blown off. The early rice was about to ripen and was all broken by the wind. The late rice was flowering, and it is unlikely to flower due to this dramatic change. Even if the seawall can be preserved, the disaster is already extremely severe.

Disaster Situation 89

Since the hurricane blew relentlessly, the Baoshan County Government immediately ordered the dike engineering technicians, dike patrolmen, and dike guards to intensify their patrols and strictly guard against danger. However, due to the excessive force of the wind, rain, and storm tides, as of yesterday (the 3rd) at noon, the sea dikes at Xuejiatan, Gulongdun, etc., had successively collapsed in more than ten places. In other places such as Laoshidong, the dike bodies were only one or two chi high in some sections, and they were all in a precarious state. The Shanghai area is in danger of being flooded like fish. It is estimated that the following dangerous situations have already occurred: ㈠ Two breaches at Xuejiatan, each two to three zhang long, with the dike body completely washed away, creating through passages. ㈡ A ten-zhang breach at the head section of Gulongdun, with the dike surface collapsed, and the most dangerous part of the dike surface only four or five chi high. ㈢ A fifteen or sixteen-zhang breach in the second section of Gulongdun, with the most severe damage, and the most dangerous part of the dike surface only one or two chi high. One place has already been breached, and water has entered. ㈣ The new works at Chenhuabin (i.e., the post-disaster rehabilitation project carried out last year), both the piles inside and the stone revetments outside the piles, have been damaged, and the dike surface is breached everywhere. ㈥ All of the emergency repair projects from the previous year at Chenhuabin and Gulongdun have been completely destroyed. ㈥ The northernmost section of the Zhangjia stone fort had the earthwork from the previous year completely washed away, and there is also a breach of about ten zhang at the end section, with the most dangerous part of the dike surface only one or two chi high. ㈦ A breach at the head section of Xuejiatan, about twenty zhang long, with the most dangerous part of the dike surface varying from three, four, or five chi high, and some sections of three or four zhang only one chi high, which is extremely dangerous. ㈧ Two layers of the dike surface at Beitang have been washed away, and more than ten or five or six stones have been damaged below. The head section of the dike surface has been washed into a channel. ㈨ More than ten wooden piles at Xiaochuanbei have been destroyed. ㈩ Four or five zhang at the southern end of the Lion Bridge have been washed away, and in the Laoshidong section, there are five or six zhang where only four or five chi of the dike body remains.

Laborers Rushing to Rescue 90

After the sea dikes in various places successively became dangerous, the Baoshan County Government, on the one hand, ordered the dike chiefs of each section to beat gongs and gather laborers to do their best to rescue, and on the other hand, hired laborers to move stones for protection. It is estimated that more than ten laborers have been recruited for the head section of Gulongdun, moving old stones to reinforce the dike. In the second section of Gulongdun, thirty or forty laborers have been recruited, and the dike chief has supervised the laborers in collecting sacks and filling the breaches. In other places, laborers are doing their best to rescue. Technicians and patrolmen are also patrolling day and night to prevent further danger.

Yesterday's Emergency Relief Association for the Yellow River Flood Released a Declaration 91

### A Lamentable Sight of Devastation Everywhere 92

### Sincere Relief to Avert Calamity 93

This newspaper has reported on the progress of the Shanghai charitable organizations that initiated the organization of the United Association for Emergency Relief for the Yellow River Flood. Declaration 94

Declaration of the United Association of Shanghai Charitable Organizations for Emergency Relief for the Yellow River Flood: It is the misfortune of the nation that disasters strike repeatedly. Since the nationwide floods of 1931, man-made and natural disasters have arisen one after another. The lamentable sight of devastation everywhere. We are mindful of the danger to the nation's foundation and the responsibility of every individual. We have repeatedly jointly initiated the Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Provincial Floods, the Shanghai War Zone Refugee Temporary Relief Association, the Shanghai Charitable Organizations United Relief Association for Northeastern Refugees, and the Shanghai Temporary Relief Association for the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Areas. We have always been grateful to compatriots at home and abroad for their tireless generosity and generous donations. However, the people suffering in the depths of water and fire have not been rescued to even a small extent, and now the Yellow River has again burst its banks. The flood has spread to the six provinces of Shandong, Henan, Shaanxi, Hebei, Anhui, and Jiangsu. The disaster area is vast, and there are many disaster victims. The huge flood reaches the sky, and cities and villages are submerged. The dead are washed away, and the living cry out. The desolation and misery, the state of danger and survival, are truly unbearable to see and hear. We are all responsible for the common good, and rescuing the hungry and weak is the duty of all. It is hoped that our elders, brothers, sisters, and all compatriots will embody the virtue of Heaven's love for life and the Buddhist spirit of universal salvation, quickly board the ship of compassion, and jointly avert this catastrophe. We, the members of this association, vow to uphold benevolence and provide sincere relief, ensuring that funds are not wasted and that our efforts are practical. All of our compatriots will truly benefit from this. We hereby declare this for your public consideration.

Current Situation in the Northeast Under Japanese Iron Heel 100

### Open Gambling and Smoking, Rampant Banditry 101

### Heavy Taxes, Impoverished People 102

The current situation in the Northeast under the Japanese iron heel is of great concern to the people of the country. The following are excerpts from a written report by a special envoy of Cheng Yun, former chairman of the Jilin Provincial Government and commander-in-chief of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army:

Open Gambling and Smoking 103

The three northeastern provinces, under the Japanese iron heel, are implementing a policy of open gambling and smoking to weaken our race. Opium sales offices and people's entertainment ticket sales offices (i.e., gambling tickets) have been established in all commercial ports, large towns, and small county towns. The situation in Harbin can be seen as an example. In Harbin, the Japanese Anti-Smoking Bureau issued opium retail licenses for a total of 36 licenses. Each license requires a deposit of 500 yuan. The opium used is sold by the Japanese Anti-Smoking Bureau at a price of 6 yuan, 6 jiao, 6 fen, and 8 li per tael. Inspectors are dispatched at any time to ensure that opium is not purchased from other sources. There are also more than 1,300 retail outlets that sell in small quantities, mostly run by Koreans. Each outlet employs two or three female attendants, each earning two to three yuan. The daily sales of opium are approximately 7,000 taels. Ten gambling licenses have been issued in Harbin, each requiring a deposit of 500 yuan. The gambling bosses then deduct 20 yuan for every 100 yuan gambled. Since the opening of opium sales, beggars have been seen everywhere, and robberies have occurred frequently, such as the two major robberies on the Gongcheng-Yushu railway line, which is unprecedented in the history of Harbin.

Forced Taxation 104

In Harbin, in addition to the customs and post office being forcibly taken over by force, navigation, salt bureau, and tax donations have also been taken over. Each county tax bureau also has a Japanese advisor. All goods imported from inland China through customs and local products are taxed an additional 30 yuan per 100 yuan, while Japanese goods are taxed only 3 yuan. Local flour produced in Harbin is taxed 5 jiao for each large bag of 150 jin and 1 jiao for each small bag.

Japanese and Puppet Troops and Police 105

Each brigade of the puppet army has several Japanese advisors, who supervise the actions of the puppet army. All books, newspapers, and official documents must be approved and signed by the Japanese before they can be issued. The armies have been reorganized by the Japanese, with each battalion changed to a three-company system, with each company having a fixed number of 80 men. Furthermore, the Harbin police security team is filling vacancies with Japanese and Koreans whenever possible. Currently, Japanese police officers account for two-tenths of the police force in Harbin.

Reorganization of the Official System 106

Each county in the eastern provinces has three Japanese officials: one is a councilor, who has the right to guide the county magistrate; one is an instructor, who can command the police; and one is the chairman of the Japanese-"Manchukuo" Cooperation Association, who has the right to guide the people. Judging from the current situation, with the exception of senior puppet officials who are willing to be puppets due to their property interests, the lower-level officers and soldiers are constantly hoping for the early restoration of the Northeast.

Current Situation of Road Administration 107

The Hulin-Hailun Railway in Heilongjiang Province has already been built. Recently, the Japanese have been extending it northward from Hailun to Heihe and building a line from Jilin to Harbin to connect with the Hulin Railway. They are currently recruiting a large number of workers to carry out the construction. A branch line is also being built from Lalin, through Fujin, to Tongjiang. This line is currently under construction. The road from Jinzhou to Rehe has been under construction for a long time, and the plan for the road from Rehe to Kulun has already been decided. All construction materials and wages are paid in puppet currency, which is also used as a means of exploiting the people. 15 million yuan has been allocated to Jilin and 10 million yuan to Jiang Province to be distributed to the people as spring plowing loans, with an annual interest rate of 8%. However, few people are willing to take out the loans, as they require land deeds as collateral, and there is a danger of confiscation after mortgaging the land.

Rampant Koreans 108

Tens of thousands of Korean households have migrated from Korea, following the Japanese army and distributing themselves in the counties east of Harbin. These Koreans seize paddy fields whenever they encounter them. Initially, the Japanese issued them a price of less than 20 yuan for every ten mu, but later they simply drove out the residents, seized the paddy fields, and did not pay any price. The Japanese army also searched the people for self-defense weapons and ordered the police to disarm. The people are furious. The people's groups in Zhuhe and Yanshou counties killed more than 280 Koreans. At the same time, 250 members of the people's groups defected and joined the anti-Japanese army of Liu Zuochen. The Japanese are immigrating Koreans to cultivate rice fields, and their purpose is primarily to supply food for the army. The northeastern armies are destroying paddy fields everywhere, not only making military food supplies hopeless but also making the immigration policy impossible to implement.

Hanging National Flags 109

Although Jilin has fallen into enemy hands, there are still places where the blue sky with a white sun flag is hung, namely the four counties of Raohe, Boli, Tongjiang, and Baoqing. These four counties are areas controlled by the anti-Japanese armies of Chen Dongshan, Wang Yong, Liang Xiangchen, Lu Yongcai, He Kuiwu, and Xie Jinglin. Later, due to the reconnaissance and bombing by seven Japanese aircraft, the blue sky with a white sun flag had to be taken down. I wonder when the national flag can be seen flying again in all parts of the Northeast.

Letter from the Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association to the Investigation Association 110

### Requesting the Chamber of Commerce to Keep and Investigate the Account Books and Receipts 111

The Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Shanghai Committee for Investigating National Salvation Donations regarding the Investigation Association's request to examine the income and expenditure account books and receipts. The two letters are recorded below.

Letter to the City Chamber of Commerce 112

Respectfully, upon receiving a letter from the Shanghai National Salvation Investigation Committee, entrusting the transfer of income and expenditure account books and receipts for settlement, the Association recognizes that the committee is a temporary group without a permanent person in charge. Should the account books and receipts be hastily delivered, the Association fears they may be scattered and lost. After investigation, the organization of the current settlement was initiated by the Association and bears significant responsibility. After deliberation, the Association decided that the account books and receipts from the date of establishment last year to August 31 of this year will be collected and sent to the Association for safekeeping and for settlement. Special envoy of the Association, accounting director Chen Weixuan, will send twenty volumes of donor registration books, two receipt books, one payment book, one general income and expenditure book, one bank deposit and withdrawal book, one hundred and fourteen receipts for revenue, and two copies of the general report on donations. We hope that each item can be checked and a receipt given.

Reply to the Investigation Committee Letter 113

Respectfully replying, previously the Association received a letter from the Committee requesting to send income and expenditure account books and receipts for settlement. The Association replied immediately to show welcome and asked that the Committee send personnel to the Association to check the accounts, should there be any unclear points that could be inquired face-to-face at any time and to provide test documents for verification and thorough investigation. On August 24, a reply letter to the Committee announced that accounting director Chen Weixuan would be responsible for contact when personnel came to check accounts. Afterward, the Committee received a letter from August 30th to have the credit record collated and sent up for review on September 1st. There was a special envoy to send the two credit records from the first and second phases, and attached forty-six pieces of donor receipt film from January to June 30th of this year for investigation and verification. The Association was waiting for the review, which was read on the same day. The reason for not being able to send personnel to review accounts was not mentioned. Instead there was a letter of approval, for reasons of inconvenience and as a matter of prudence, there was difficulty sending, refusal to settle and further deep regret, and so on. The letter sent to the Association stated reasons that were not in conformity, and said the settlement was rejected, the opinion was completely contrary to the idea of repeated settlement, and truly deeply horrified. It was also stated that income and expenditure during the settlement period should be stopped immediately, which overran the settlement range, interfered with the main work of the Association, and was difficult to acknowledge. The Association eagerly awaits the settlement, which is the same as the Committee's intention. How the wording of the letter should be, we will leave for now. Only if account books and receipts were instructed to be submitted for review, it was not stated when they should be sent and who should receive them. The Association, as a temporary collective, in the event of loss of important receipts, who should be responsible in the future? After investigating the organizational elements of the Committee, the Association was led by the Chamber of Commerce, so the Association decided to send the income and expenditure account books and receipts to the Chamber of Commerce for safekeeping and for settlement. In addition to the letter sent to the Chamber of Commerce, a corresponding letter replied in hopes of the check.

Shanghai Zhabei Silk Factory Workers Negotiate Resumption of Work on the 5th 114

### Production Quota System Awaits Mediation 115

The Shanghai silk factory workers oppose the implementation of the production quota system. After the strike occurred in seventeen silk factories including Zhabei Xinzha area Baotai, the union and the trade association directly negotiated the night before last, and it has come to an end. The production quota system will be postponed for one month, and the striking factories will resume work on the 5th. Here are the details:

Actual Number of Strikers 116

A reporter from Xin Sheng She went to investigate the situation of the striking factories in order to understand the situation. It is known that there are a total of twenty-seven silk factories including Baotai in the Xinzha area that have started work, and four including Ruilun. The four were originally scheduled to start operations on September 1, but in view of the opposition of the workers at factories such as Baotai, they temporarily suspended operations. On the 1st, twelve factories including Baotai went on strike. On the morning of the 2nd, seven of the twelve factories that went on strike stopped sounding the steam whistle to start work. Five factories started work, but the workers did not enter the factory to resume work, and then stopped work immediately. In the afternoon, the female workers of five factories including Xinda were affected by the strike, for a total of seventeen factories. The reporter went to inquire about Mr. Shen Huachen, chairman of the trade association, and learned that the factories on strike in the news area were indeed seventeen, and the rumors of thirty-three are inaccurate.

Continued Shutdown 117

Dagon She says that since fourteen factories including Baotai on Changan Road in Zhabei announced a joint strike on the afternoon of the 1st of this month, the situation has become quite serious when the factories in the Xinzha District and the concession area were also affected the day before yesterday. Yesterday was Sunday, and the factories were closed as usual, so the steam whistle was not sounded in the morning. Today is also the Ghost Festival in the old calendar, which is also a holiday for silk factories, so all factories are closed.

Labor-Management Negotiation 118

The Shanghai Silk Industry Union of various districts believes that the silk factories in Zhabei have caused the workers' reaction due to the change to the production quota system, and a strike has occurred. They are deeply concerned that the conflict will expand and affect the silk factories throughout the city, so they specially sent directors Yang Gengdi, Yuan Yunlong, Chen Xiupu, Wu Suzhen, etc. to negotiate with Shen Huachen, chairman of the trade association, and asked them to postpone the implementation of the production quota system and form a research committee to conduct research before implementing it. As a result of the consultation, both parties have reached a considerable understanding, and it has been decided that all factories will sound the steam whistle to start work tomorrow morning. The workers will be persuaded to resume work by the union.

Party and Government Instructions 119

The Shanghai Party and government agencies immediately sent personnel to investigate the truth after hearing about the joint strike of silk factory workers in Zhabei. They believe that although this labor conflict occurred because the factory changed to the production quota system, the workers went on strike suddenly before reporting to the Party and government for mediation, which is not the case. Therefore, it was decided that the Municipal Party Department and the Social Bureau would jointly instruct the silk unions in various districts to immediately persuade the workers to resume work. The issue of changing to the production quota system will be studied again before formally mediating between the two parties.

Notice of Resumption of Work 120

The Shanghai Sixth District Silk Industry Union issued a notice to the workers of each factory yesterday, that all workers should enter the factory to resume work tomorrow morning, and wait for the Party and government to resolve the issue of the production quota system in accordance with the law. The notice is recorded as follows: Notice: Due to the unauthorized implementation of the production quota system by the factories, the workers of the silk factories in Xinzha District of this district have announced a strike. This association has joined forces with the unions of the third and fourth districts to formulate measures and request the Party and government authorities to be fair and reasonable, and order the factories to postpone the implementation of the production quota system. If the silk factories have indeed postponed the implementation, all workers should enter the factory to resume work, otherwise they should wait for a solution and refrain from extra-curricular actions. It is of utmost importance to comply with this notice.

Declaration 121

The joint declaration of the silk industry trade unions of various cities and districts regarding the factory's adoption of the output system states: In recent years, China's foreign trade in raw silk has plummeted, approaching failure. Although the reason for this is partly due to the pressure from Japanese silk, it is undeniable that Chinese silk has not sought improvement. Therefore, if we want to restore the position of Chinese silk in the international market today, improving the manufacturing of raw silk is an urgent and essential task. Our unions absolutely agree in principle with the factory's proposed adoption of an output system. However, upon closer examination of its content, it is impossible not to have doubts. On August 29th, our unions received notice from the factory that the output system would be implemented on September 1st. The urgency of the timing left no opportunity for consideration, which violates the spirit of the mediation record signed on July 8th. Moreover, the so-called output system this time was neither agreed upon by our unions beforehand, nor was there a specific plan or a defined work standard. Furthermore, it is said that although the maximum wage is slightly increased based on the current quota (only increased by four percent), there is a limit that cannot be exceeded. Therefore, no matter how hard-working and skilled the workers are, they cannot receive the wages they deserve due to the limit of the maximum amount. On the other hand, there is no limit to the reduction of wages for those with lower work efficiency. This kind of unfair method is not an output system, but a disguised wage reduction. It can be seen that the original intention of implementing the output system to improve the silk industry, to encourage workers, and to increase work efficiency is probably not like this. Therefore, our unions believe that if the factory is truly determined to improve the silk industry, it should immediately postpone the implementation of this unilaterally decided output system. At the same time, both labor and management should each appoint several representatives to form a research committee under the supervision of party and government agencies. The committee should study based on the principles of developing production, labor-management mutual benefit, and determine a proper plan for the implementation of the output system, specific standards, and other methods of improvement. Only then will there be hope for the revival of the silk industry. This is what our unions earnestly hope for. This declaration is hereby made.
