The Center of the Hurricane Has Not Reached Shanghai and Has Already Blown to Southern Korea Yesterday 132

=The Losses in Various Places Are Not as Severe as in 1931=

=Cotton and Late Rice Were Most Severely Damaged Due to Wind and Rain Immersion=

丨Yesterday the Wind Force Decreased Greatly and Ships Exported as Usual丨

When the hurricane passed through Huadao and Shanbei Island the night before, the port was also affected, resulting in losses in the South City, Zhabei, West Shanghai, Pudong, and Wusong areas. However, it was not as severe as in 1931. Yesterday, the hurricane had changed direction and blown to Southern Korea. The wind labor in the port gradually weakened, and ships have been exporting as usual. The situation is recorded as follows:

Port Affected 133

According to the explanation of the Observatory, the center of the hurricane never passed through Shanghai. Although the wind force in the port was strong last night, it was only affected by the edge of the hurricane. The hurricane did come directly towards Shanghai on the afternoon of the 2nd. However, at 4 o'clock the night before, when it reached 30 degrees north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude, it suddenly changed direction. Therefore, the hurricane did not land, and its center did not pass through Shanghai. At about 9 o'clock the night before, it passed through the border of Huadao and Shanbei Island, so the wind force there reached a huge 12 on the Beaufort scale. The area is only 60 miles away from Shanghai, so there were gales of 10 on the Beaufort scale in the port that night. By 6 o'clock yesterday morning, the hurricane had reached 32 degrees north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude, which is about 90 miles away from Shanghai.

Heading to Korea 134

At 6 o'clock yesterday morning, the hurricane changed from the north-northwest direction to the north-northeast direction. At that time, there was a tendency to attack Korea. By 4 p.m., when the center of the hurricane reached 33 degrees north latitude and 125 degrees east longitude, it changed to a northeast direction. At that time, according to the report of the Observatory, it was obvious that it was blowing to Southern Korea. There are cyclones and tidal waves in the Korean Sea, and heavy gales in the Yellow Sea. According to the exploration, the wind force in the port was 10 on the Beaufort scale the night before, and decreased to 8 yesterday morning. It will be further reduced at night. In addition, Huadao and Shanbei Island outside the Wusongkou had a wind force of 12 the night before, which was reduced to 9 yesterday morning, and reduced to 8 in the afternoon.

Getting Better at Night 135

According to the report issued by the Observatory yesterday afternoon, the climate in the port is cooler, with light and calm showers and gales, but it will gradually improve at night. The hurricane is more inclined to the northeast and is proceeding to Southern Korea. There are cyclones and tidal waves in the Korean Sea, and heavy gales in the Yellow Sea. It was also learned that the wind force in the port was 10 the night before, which decreased to 8 yesterday morning, and will be further reduced at night. In addition, Huadao and Shanbei Island outside the Wusongkou had a wind force of 12 the night before, which was reduced to 9 yesterday morning, and reduced to 8 in the afternoon.

Ships Exporting 136

After the hurricane passed, the wind force has gradually subsided, and ships in the port have been exporting as usual. According to reports, the ships that exported yesterday were the Kalemulan, Nagasaki Maru, Wusong, Fusheng, Tongzhou, Fusheng, Xinning, and Carl Kies. The imports were the Lailai Wensi, Longhe, and Xiyang Maru, etc., totaling seven or eight ships.

Losses in Various Places 137

It is reported that when the hurricane affected Shanghai the night before, there were many losses in various parts of the port. In the South City area, such as the Nanyang Iron Factory on Bansongyuan Road, the perimeter wall more than ten feet long was blown down by the gale. At the same time, the front walls of houses No. 56, 57, and 58 in the Fifth Lane of Furunli, Jiumu Land in the city, and the high walls of No. 66, 67, 68, 69, and 70, and the high perimeter wall of the Supervision Department of the Municipal Public Security Bureau also collapsed. The awnings of various wharves on the Bund were also blown away. Many telephone and electric light lines were blown down. Yesterday morning, the Huashang Electric Company and the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications sent a large number of workers to repair them separately. It is expected that they can be restored to their original state on the same day. The Wenmiao Park suffered great losses after the gale and rainstorm the night before. Seventy percent of the trees in the entire park were broken. All the street light electric lines in the park were broken. The roofs of several places were damaged due to the trees falling on them. In addition, the Municipal Zoo also suffered losses, but not much. In addition, there were also considerable losses in Pudong and West Shanghai. In the Zhabei area, many Jiangbei grass sheds were blown down and collapsed, resulting in considerable losses.

Water Receded and Cars Passed 138

At 9 o'clock the night before, the wind was tight and the tide was high, causing Huangpu South Road, Sichuan Road, Jiangxi Road, Henan Road, etc. to be gradually submerged. It was not until 7 o'clock yesterday morning that the water began to recede slightly. Zhejiang Road, Hubei Road, Hankou Road, and the area between Nanjing Road had lower elevations, so the water receded more slowly. The streetcars were blocked and stopped. The open space in front of the Wing On Company, which had already started construction, was filled with mud and soil due to pile driving, so the water depth reached six feet. The houses in Tianbaoli, Xinjiang Road, were all submerged by eight inches of water. It was not until about 2 p.m. that the water receded completely and the tracks appeared. However, the tracks were filled with mud, so the streetcar company ordered workers to remove it. At the same time, the No. 3 and No. 6 streetcars of the British Streetcar Company and the No. 5 streetcars of the French Water and Electricity Company were all opened.

Increase Ferry 139

Although the wind force yesterday was not as strong as the day before, the yin and yang were combined, and there were light showers. The waves in the Huangpu River were high and the tide was rapid. The ferry sampans in the Huangpu River temporarily announced price increases due to the strong winds and rapid tides. The usual ferry boat fare was increased from 40 to 60 per person, and the sampan fare was increased from 10 cents to 20 cents. Moreover, from west to east, due to the headwind, it took an hour, so most people changed to the city ferry at Dongmen Road. The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau temporarily opened the No. 12 ferry at Dongchang Road and Dongmen Road, because the ferry was crowded with passengers and prone to danger.

Losses in West Shanghai 140

Various places in West Shanghai suffered considerable losses from the hurricane and rainstorm from the night before to yesterday morning. The following is a record of what was seen and heard: ㈠ The lights went out. At about 2 o'clock yesterday morning, the power lines in the Zhoujiaqiao area were blown down, and the lights went out completely. There were sparks shooting out from the power lines from time to time, and the larger ones fell like fireballs. The general residents were all frightened and hid. Several power lines were also broken in the Caojiadu Jessfield Road area, and all the lights were out. The lights in the Sixth District Office also went out. Fortunately, District Chief Tan took precautions early and used gas lamps instead. The residents were sleeping soundly, so there was no problem. ㈠ Grass sheds collapsed. Dozens of grass sheds inhabited by poor Jiangbei people in Zhoujiaqiao, Bangbei Tan Zitao, Zhongshan Road, Tanjiadu, Robison Road, and other places were blown down and damaged. It was heard that a grass shed in Tanzi Bay housed four people, large and small. At 3 o'clock yesterday morning, it suddenly collapsed, injuring an old woman and a child. Their heads were broken and bleeding, and their injuries were serious. The grass sheds collapsed and broke, and the poor people cried and ran away like chickens in the water. The situation was pitiful. In addition, the mat sheds and bamboo fences of the residents on Jessfield Road, Connaught Road, and Yuyuan Road were also blown down everywhere. ㈠ Trees were blown down. There were four or five trees on Yuyuan Road, two trees on Jiaozhou Road, about seven or eight trees on Rue Say-Zoong, and five trees at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Chongqing Road. A large tree was blown down at the Chenjiazhai near Zhongshan Road. ㈠ Billboards collapsed. Four large pieces of the large billboard next to the Jing'an Temple were damaged. Three large pieces were knocked down at the intersection of Avenue Foch and Tongfu Road. ㈠ Agricultural losses. In the farmlands of West Shanghai, the planted rice, cotton, beans, etc. were mostly blown down. According to the farmers, the rice and cotton were greatly affected, and the future harvest will be greatly discounted.

What Was Seen and Heard in Pudong 141

After the port suffered a hurricane the day before, the large and small boats in the Huangpu River were suspended due to the huge waves. The city ferry between Dongdou Road in Puxi and Dongchang Road in Pudong was suspended at 5 pm to avoid danger, resulting in the complete isolation of news from Pudong. People who work in Puxi could not take a boat home and had to borrow rooms in nearby hotels. Those who lived in Puxi but worked in Pudong also stayed in Pudong and could not cross the river. The general situation of Pudong suffering from the hurricane and heavy rain is recorded as follows: On the day before, because the wind was weak, the residents did not take it seriously. By 8 or 9 pm, the wind became stronger and the rain was pouring down. The streets were deserted and became desolate. At about 11 pm, the Pudong water landed and passed over several miles. The water on Dongchang Road was knee-deep, and those with low houses were all flooded. All places became a vast ocean. And the electricity poles on the streets were blown down by the strong wind. In order to prevent danger, the Pudong Electric Company closed the main hub, so the lights were all turned off. In this dark world, the residents became more panicked. The sound of crying could be heard everywhere. Fortunately, after 1:30 am, the water gradually receded, and it completely receded at 3 am, so they could sleep peacefully. After the reporter waited for dawn, he went to various places to investigate and saw that the bamboo fences were blown down everywhere, and many large trees were also uprooted. There were also a large number of Jiangbei shantytowns that were blown down, and the Jiangbei people were homeless and in a very pitiful state. The Pudong Electric Company ordered a large team of workers to repair the poles and lines in various places throughout the morning, so the power was restored normally in the afternoon. The city ferry at the Dongchang Road Wharf operated normally yesterday morning in order to take care of the east-west traffic relations in Puxi.

Also, at about 2 o'clock yesterday morning, when the waves were churning in the Huangpu River, a pier boat of Zhou Miaosheng, loaded with 42 pieces of white iron, was moored at the Ningshao Wharf in the Sixteenth Concession. It was suddenly overturned by a big wave, and the goods were completely submerged at the bottom of the river. The hull of the boat also drifted away. At 2 p.m. yesterday, Zhou requested the Customs Water Patrol Room to file a case. It was heard that the goods were declared by the Lichang Public Customs Brokerage on Sijing Road, Public Concession.

Wusong Situation 142

Wusong bore the brunt of the hurricane's outbreak. From the day before to the night of yesterday, merchant ships were blown over, roads were breached by huge waves, and rice was damaged. The details are recorded as follows: ㈠ The tide rose sharply. When the hurricane came, it happened to be the northeast wind, so the tide rose sharply with the wind, the waves rose and fell, and the huge waves were torrential. The tide in the Yunzao Creek was level with the outer road. In the afternoon, the northeast wind blew tighter and tighter, causing the tide to not recede all day. The evening tide was even greater, rushing to the road. At that time, the Yangjiazhai area on the south bank of Yunzao Creek became a swamp, and the houses of the people were flooded with more than three or four feet of water, even the pots on the stove were floated away. There were four or five floating coffins behind the houses. Fortunately, the wind turned to the old north wind with the west from 10 pm, so the tide did not progress any further. Otherwise, it would be unimaginable. However, the highest tide had risen to more than 40 feet on the Customs water ruler. ㈠ Merchant ships were blown over. The Jiangbei Tianshenggang pig boat Jinchangfa, loaded with 195 live pigs, came to Shanghai to sell. At 10 pm the night before, it sailed into the Sanjia Shuikou in Wusong and was stranded on the stone embankment by a hurricane, causing the entire ship to capsize, and the bottom of the ship was also pierced. Later, the pig customer rushed to report to Mr. Hong Wenjiang, director of the Wusong Delivery Office of the Shanghai Fresh Pig Industry, who immediately hired the Zhongxing tugboat to rescue the live pigs, and all of them were discharged in Wusong. More than a dozen crew members and pig customers were rescued. The ship was badly damaged. There was also a Gaoqiao ferry whose mast was broken by the wind and was about to capsize. Fortunately, it was rescued by another ship, so more than a dozen ferry passengers were spared from drowning. It is heard that there were many other pig boats and merchant ships outside the Sanjia Watergate that were blown over and damaged by the hurricane. Currently, no reports have been received, so there is no way to find out the names of the ships. ㈠ The road was breached. The eastern section of the Wusong Road is the most important place for tidal ebb and flow, so a cement stone embankment was built along the Bund to protect the roadbed. The tide increased sharply the night before, and the huge waves rushed and broke the embankment in five or six places, the larger ones being four or five feet and the smaller ones being one or two feet. However, the place is the key point of the whole town of Wusong, so the situation is quite dangerous. Yesterday, the Municipal Public Works Bureau sent workers to rush to repair it and used bamboo fences and mud to build a temporary emergency method. ㈠ Rice fields were damaged. The rice fields near Wusong suffered great damage during the hurricane. Because the early rice has matured and can be harvested soon, the rice stalks were blown down by the hurricane, and the tide rose sharply, turning the fields into swamps. After a long period of time, the rice will be immersed in water and will inevitably germinate. The late rice is in the fruiting period, and it is feared that there will be no hope for the future harvest after this huge blow. The amount of loss is difficult to estimate.

㈠ Affecting traffic. The Songhu branch line of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, from Zhanghuabang to Fort Taiwan, was also affected by the hurricane. The entire line was flooded the night before, causing traffic to be temporarily suspended yesterday morning. It did not resume operation until the water receded at 11 a.m. yesterday.

Fraud Case of Less Than Sixty Yuan

Wrapping Paper Scams Banknotes 143

Renting a Guest Room as a Crime Site

Owner of a Copper Coin Exchange Shop Deceived

The world is getting worse, people's hearts are not ancient, and the fraud dramas that occur in society are becoming more and more strange and wonderful. Yesterday, a fraud case of using toilet paper to scam banknotes worth 60 yuan occurred in the South City. Although the purpose of the fraud was small, the cunning of the fraud was unexpected. The details of the case obtained from the investigation are recorded as follows:

Starting to Ask for Exchange 144

Dashun Cigarette Exchange Shop, No. 115 Fusantang Street, outside Xiaonanmen, South City, has a fairly prosperous business on weekdays. On the 1st of this month, a man of about 30 years old, speaking in a Ningbo accent, suddenly went to the shop and claimed that he was a dealer in copper coins and wondered if the shop wanted copper coins. The shop owner said that the copper coins in the shop were still usable, so he replied that he did not. The man then said goodbye and left. The next day (2nd), the man came again to inquire, and the shop owner still replied that the shop was not short of copper coins and left.

Negotiating the Price 145

Unexpectedly, at about 9 a.m. yesterday, the man went to the Dashun Cigarette Exchange Shop again and claimed that he had more than 200,000 copper coins at home, and the exchange rate was low. He did not know if the shop wanted to exchange some. The shop owner said that the shop was indeed short of copper coins, and the man had come twice in a row, so it was difficult to refuse. He replied that 200,000 copper coins was too much. Now the shop only needs to exchange 60 yuan of copper coins. The man readily agreed. After the two sides negotiated the price of exchanging 300 copper coins per silver dollar, the man said that all his copper coins were at home. He asked them to send someone to take them with him. The shop owner sent an apprentice, Weng Jinfu (16 years old, from Sanbei), to follow the man with 60 yuan of banknotes to exchange copper coins.

Accompanied to the Guest Room 146

Before long, the two arrived at No. 8 Tongjili, Qinglong Bridge. The man opened the door and entered, and the apprentice Weng Jinfu also followed him inside. He saw dozens of packages of copper coins in the guest room, shaped like 2,000 packages each. All of them were wrapped in old newspapers. Weng stepped forward and took a package from the top. He felt that what was wrapped inside was indeed copper coins. Just as he was about to count the number of packages, the man called out repeatedly, "Don't move, don't move! There are a total of one hundred silver dollars of copper coins here. How much do you want to exchange? You can tell me, and I can give it to you." Weng replied that he wanted to exchange 60 silver dollars of copper coins. The man asked for the silver dollars, and Weng handed over all 60 yuan of banknotes to the man.

Abrupt Disappearance 147

That person immediately said, "Sixty foreign coins can be exchanged for many copper coins that you alone cannot carry. Now, you go outside first and call for a rickshaw, and have it wait at the entrance. I will wait here, and after you call for the rickshaw, I will hand over the exchanged copper coins to you and help you load them onto the rickshaw to take back to the shop." Old Weng agreed and went out. Soon, he hired a rickshaw and returned to the original place, but that person had already disappeared. He then automatically moved the paper packages placed in the parlor onto the rickshaw. Suddenly, he felt that the contents of the six paper packages on top were indeed copper coins, totaling twelve thousand. However, the dozens of packages piled underneath felt very light in weight. When he squeezed them, they didn't feel like copper coins either, and he immediately became suspicious. He then opened each one to inspect them, only to discover that all the items rolled up inside these paper packages were toilet paper.

Incriminating the Second Landlord 148

Upon seeing this, the apprentice was greatly alarmed and hurriedly looked around, but the person had already vanished without a trace. He then realized that he had been deceived. He rushed back to the shop and reported to the shop owner, who immediately ordered the apprentice to return to the place and bring back the six packages of real copper coins (totaling twelve thousand) to the shop. Then, he went to the place again and, together with Yuan Zhi, the police officer on duty at the 31st Precinct, took the dozens of paper packages resembling copper coins, as well as the toilet paper inside and the second landlord of the house, Han Yun-die, to the First Precinct's First Station. It was already past noon at that time.

Han Yun-die's Testimony 149

When the station chief, Yi Zuan-ren, conducted a preliminary interrogation, the apprentice, Weng Jin-fu, recounted the previous events and requested a thorough investigation. Han Yun-die testified that she was twenty years old, from Huzhou, and lived at 8 Tongji Lane. She had previously studied at Junyi Middle School, but dropped out and joined the Sincere Company as a female clerk in the fountain pen department. After only three months due to the workload being too heavy, she quit her job and stayed at home. Recently, she had come to Shanghai from her hometown to prepare for the entrance exam to Wuben Girls' Middle School this semester. Recently, there was a parlor on the ground floor of her house that she was planning to rent out, so she had posted a "For Rent" sign at the entrance.

Pretext of Renting a Room 150

Yesterday (the day before yesterday) at around 2 PM, a person, about thirty years old and speaking with a Ningbo accent, wearing a blue-gray silk long gown, came to view the parlor on the ground floor. After deeming it satisfactory, they agreed on a monthly rent of nine and a half foreign coins. That person immediately paid a deposit of one foreign coin and claimed to work on a ship and also trade copper coins. After that person left, they came to my house at around 6 AM this morning (yesterday), bringing two wooden boxes containing dozens of paper packages that looked exactly like copper coins. We didn't suspect anything because he had claimed the day before that he traded copper coins. That person then said that these copper coins would be temporarily placed in the parlor and moved upstairs when his family members came to move in the afternoon. Because he was already a tenant, we immediately agreed.

Truly Not in Conspiracy 151

That person then bid farewell and left. Not long after, he brought an apprentice to come and move the copper coins. We didn't pay much attention until later when the apprentice realized that the packages contained a scam and the swindler had already escaped without a trace and could not be apprehended. Therefore, that person used toilet paper to swindle cash, and we were truly not in conspiracy with him. I hope you will investigate carefully. As the matter concerned a swindling case, he ordered her to be temporarily detained while he dispatched police officers to investigate the truth before further action was taken.

Agricultural Medical Society Sends Personnel to Zhejiang 152

Investigating the Real Situation of Eleutherococcus and Fritillaria Cooperation

Zhejiang fritillaria is one of the main domestic medicinal materials. The annual output is enormous and sold throughout the country. Farmers in Xiangshan, Yinjiang, and other places rely on planting this medicinal herb to make a living. In recent years, it has transformed from a superior sideline into the backbone of the rural economy. Since the organization of the Xiangshan Eleutherococcus and Fritillaria Marketing Cooperative in March this year, a cooperative sales monopoly has been implemented. Recently, the pharmaceutical markets in Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, Beijing, and other places have felt uneasy due to the sudden increase in the price of Eleutherococcus and Fritillaria. Some even suspect that the cooperative has lost its original intention of organization. To thoroughly understand the real situation of Eleutherococcus and Fritillaria production and the overview of marketing cooperation, the Rural Medical Improvement Society has specially sent the director-general, Zhu Dian, and staff member Xu Gongyu to Ningbo by boat tonight to conduct an on-the-spot investigation to improve the situation.

Tram Service Planned for Downtown Area

Otherwise, not only would western Shanghai be able to prosper, but transportation between Shanghai and Wusong could also be greatly facilitated. As for the construction of the Qiujiang Pier to facilitate cargo transportation, it is still in the planning stage due to funding constraints. The opening of a public bus route in the city center area requires the Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company to expand its capital due to capital constraints to facilitate its progress. In the future, official shares may need to be added to achieve joint official-private management.

Page 13

Municipal Public Security Bureau Police Brigade Renamed General Brigade 155

Approved by the Municipal Government

The organizational laws of public security bureaus in various provinces and cities originally established security teams or security brigades. However, due to special circumstances in this city, there is a separate Security Office under the jurisdiction of the Municipal Government. To avoid duplication, the Municipal Public Security Bureau changed the name of the Security Team to the Police Brigade. However, this was not fully in accordance with the army's organizational law. Therefore, Director Wen presented the organizational content and reasons to the Municipal Government for approval. The mayor then approved the renaming of the original Police Brigade to the Police General Brigade, without establishing separate brigades. The original squadrons will remain as they were. The Bureau has already notified all districts and stations under its jurisdiction of this order.

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Drafts Fish Market Plan 156

Submitted to the Municipal Government for Transfer to the Ministry of Industry for Approval

Total Construction Cost of One Million Yuan

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau recently drafted a plan for the Shanghai Fish Market and submitted it to the Municipal Government for transfer to the Ministry of Industry for approval. The original draft plan is excerpted as follows:

(A) Equipment of the Shanghai Fish Market: (1) Special wharf for fisheries: This wharf must be at least 600 feet long, built along the shore, with a floating ship attached that can rise and fall with the tide. This is to allow the city's fishing boats, refrigerated fish boats, and freshwater fish boats to dock and unload their catches at any time, and to load ice and coal. This will enable two trawlers and many refrigerated fish boats and freshwater fish boats to dock at the same time, so that loading and unloading can be done quickly and time can be saved. (2) Cold storage and ice-making plant: The cold storage facility must have a volume of at least 100,000 cubic feet to store a large quantity of aquatic products. The ice-making plant must be able to produce 40 tons of ice per day to supply fishing boats and refrigerated boats. (3) Packaging yard and warehouse: The packaging yard is used to sort and organize the catch after it is unloaded. The packaging yard will handle products that are supplied to the market, are to be imported inland, or are to be stored in cold storage in advance to ensure speed. The warehouse will be used to store salted and dried aquatic products. (4) Auction hall: The auction hall is an important place for the fish market to operate every morning. The area must be large, and the ventilation, lighting, and wastewater disposal system must be carefully designed. The layout should be in a grid pattern to facilitate traffic inside the hall, and it can be designed with reference to the construction method of small vegetable markets. (5) Fisheries Bank: As the fish market is the only collection and distribution center for fresh and salted fish in the city, it is estimated that the total monthly turnover is about 1.5 million yuan. Loans for operating advances and for fishermen and fish merchants are inevitable. For the sake of circulating finance and prospering the fishing industry, the establishment of a fisheries bank is particularly important. (6) Fisheries consumer cooperative: All the supplies needed for fisheries and the daily needs of fishermen, whether for business or personal consumption, are usually purchased through intermediaries, whose exploitation is quite considerable over the years. Therefore, it is necessary to establish a consumer cooperative to purchase and consume together, which can eliminate the profit-sharing of intermediaries and save expenses and increase income. (7) Preparation of refrigerated trucks and refrigerated ships: The purpose of establishing a fish market is to regulate food for the people, promote production, and promote sales. However, in the event of overproduction or strong demand from other ports, in addition to using the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways and Yangtze River ships for transportation to other ports, towns and villages closer to the fish market must use roads for transportation in refrigerated trucks. Conversely, in the event of insufficient supply, it is necessary to prepare fresh-collecting ships and refrigerated ships to go to the fishing grounds to collect fresh fish. (8) Live fish pond: Shanghai's annual consumption of freshwater fish imports is no less than 5 million yuan, and most of the fish comes from places such as Linghu, Zhejiang. Usually, after the live fish boats arrive in Shanghai, they cannot leave Shanghai until they are completely sold, which is time-consuming and uneconomical. Therefore, the fish market must prepare its own live fish pond for short-term breeding. (9) Telecommunications equipment: In order to communicate with the fishing grounds, the fish market should be equipped with a 100-watt short-wave radio station to communicate with the fishing boats working in the fishing grounds and report the market price of various fish every day, so that each fishing boat can independently budget the value of its catch to determine the date of import. (10) Entertainment Department: Including reading newspapers, reading books, bathing, movies, lecture halls, etc. (11) Offices of various departments of the fish market. (12) Dormitory.

(B) Location of the fish market: Since the Greater Shanghai Plan was determined, efforts have been made to construct the central area. In the future, when the commercial port moves north and the railway moves far away, the concession will no longer be able to be the hub of the whole city, and citizens may move. The construction of the fish market should be close to the commercial port area, near Wusong Yunzaobang, which seems to be more appropriate. The realization of this commercial port plan will take time, so if the Shanghai Fish Market needs to be built in the next year or two, it may still be appropriate to choose a site near the Guanqiao area of Nanshi along the shore. However, in order to facilitate the control of incoming and outgoing fishing boats so that they are not monopolized by old forces, building the fish market north of Yangshupu and close to the urban center along the shore can be a powerful control measure.

(C) Business Scope and Business Methods of the Shanghai Fish Market: Before the central government promulgates the Fish Market Law, the organization and business of the fish market will be handled in accordance with the draft Fish Market Law. The fish market is the highest authority in the local area to control aquatic products, fresh and salted fish, and bears a heavy responsibility. Its business scope includes not only seafood and river fish but also dried products. The business method is mainly entrusted sales in the ordinary department. It accepts the entrustment of fishing vessels, ice-fresh vessels, salt-fresh vessels, and river-fresh vessels to sell on their behalf. When there is a shortage of market demand and entrusted purchases from the mainland, it must find ways to purchase them itself to regulate the catch. In order to regulate the catch, the fish market first organizes packaging to sort out the catch and estimate the quantity of daily food needed by the city's residents. If the products are to be sold to the mainland or there are orders, they will be packaged and shipped to the mainland by the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways and Yangtze River ships. Therefore, from the very beginning of its establishment, the fish market must contact the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways and the China Merchants Bureau to add refrigerated equipment to facilitate transportation. Those towns and villages near the city that do not have railways or ships will be transported by refrigerated trucks or refrigerated ships. If there is still fish left, it will be stored in cold storage. (Omitted in the middle) The wholesale of fresh and salted fish in the fish market is sold by brokers by auction. After the auction is completed, the person in charge of the fish market will hand over the fish price to the seller, deducting only a small handling fee. The rate is from 5% of the selling price and shall not exceed 7%.

(D) Funds: The construction cost includes 200,000 yuan for the construction of the entire fish market, another 200,000 yuan for the cold storage and ice-making plant, about 100,000 yuan for the wharf and refrigerated trucks and ships, and 500,000 yuan for the Fisheries Bank capital, totaling 1 million yuan. However, the land value is not included.

Chronicle of the New Huizhou Association's Gathering 160

Yu Hongjun Speaks on the Benefits of Joining the Fellow Countrymen Association

The New Huizhou Association held a gathering at Apricot Blossom House on Fourth Ma Road yesterday at 6:00 PM. Dozens of people attended. Zhao Chaochang, chairman, announced the purpose of the meeting, followed by Executive Committee member Zheng Xingpu reporting on the progress of the association's affairs. Municipal Government Secretary General Yu Hongjun was also present yesterday. His speech was summarized as follows: "Your enthusiasm for the association's affairs is admirable. However, there are no less than 10,000 fellow countrymen, and less than 5% have joined the association. This is because everyone is looking out for themselves and sees no difference between joining or not joining the association. I believe that for oneself and for others, one must join the fellow countrymen association. The saying goes, 'Watch out for each other and help each other in times of illness.' If you join, you will have the association's duty to provide guidance for seeing a doctor, receiving education, or in the event of an accident, which can avoid all kinds of difficulties. If the New Huizhou Association occupies a superior position in society, any problem will be easy to deal with. It is not just about joining the association, paying membership fees, and having dinners. Look at the achievements of the Ningbo Fellow Countrymen Association. It has been able to deal with the Northeast issue and government issues. We should use our brains, think more, and jointly organize basic methods to recognize the center of gravity. If lawyers, doctors, artists, architects, and business people all look out for themselves, they will not have a strong organization. As for the current New Huizhou Association's grave sweeping and dinners, all the proceedings cannot go beyond the scope of the past fellow countrymen associations. We should look at the Shanghai environment and the government's position to strive for survival and first seek the establishment of basic institutions before we have a foothold. Fellow countrymen should broaden their horizons, focus on efforts, and seek happiness for the masses, not just limit themselves to charity and education."

Official Deed Required for Buying and Pledging Real Estate 161

The Shanghai County Government issued a notice yesterday, stating: "According to an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, 'This department has previously drafted measures for township and town offices in various counties to assist in deed taxation, and is hereby ordered to be followed. Please notify the citizens of the county so that they are aware that in the future, when encountering matters of buying and pledging real estate, they must purchase official deed paper from the relevant township and town office nearby to write the deed and submit it to the county for taxation within the time limit. Private paper deeds must no longer be used, or they will be punished.' The case involves the reorganization of deed tax and essential measures, which must not be ignored.' Having received this order, in addition to ordering all districts to forward it to the various townships and towns for compliance, it is hereby announced to the citizens of the county so that they are aware that when adding property, they must obtain the protection of the law. If they greedily conceal it and privately use blank deeds, if discovered, not only will they lose its legal effect, but they will also be severely punished. The gains and losses are not difficult to choose. The purpose of the Department's order is not only to boost tax revenue, but also to stabilize property rights for all industries. Everyone must understand this intention. Whenever they encounter matters of selling and pledging real estate, they must purchase official deed paper from the relevant township and town offices nearby to write the deed. There must be no mistakes."

A Woman Commits Suicide After Being Wronged by a Neighbor 162

Wu Mingcai, a Chongming native from 9 Zhujiazhai, Houfu North Road, behind the new municipal government in the city center of East Shanghai, worked as a hired laborer there and lived with his wife and children. His wife, Wu Wang-shi, was 35 years old and a traditional woman from the countryside with a narrow mind who liked to gossip with neighbors. More than ten days ago, she had a quarrel with a neighbor over a trivial matter. The neighbor was eloquent, so in the end, Wu Wang-shi was no match in the village women's scolding match. Her face turned red, she felt ashamed, and returned home. She could not vent her anger and cried alone. When her husband returned home and saw this situation, he was very surprised and asked what was wrong. She then told him the whole story, hoping that her husband would stand up for her. However, Wu was a lonely stranger in a foreign land and a hired laborer, and he did not have the ability to do so. He did not dare to interfere too much, so he warned his wife not to be meddlesome. She was even more saddened that her husband did not help her but instead blamed her, and she grieved that she had married a cowardly and incompetent husband, causing his wife and children to suffer. When Wu saw this, he tried to comfort her in every way possible, and she temporarily stopped crying, but she remained depressed, as if she had a lot on her mind and had nowhere to vent it. Yesterday afternoon, her husband went to work in the fields. When he returned home, he could not find his wife and called out but received no response. He searched the room and found that she had hanged herself on the bedrail. He quickly untied her, but she had been dead for a long time. Wu was distraught by this tragedy and reported to the 7th District, 1st Station, requesting justice for his wife. He was instructed to have the local Baojia chief report for examination first. Ouyang Shu, a prosecutor from the local court, went to the scene to examine the body and confirmed that she had committed suicide by hanging. He ordered the body to be taken for burial and await further investigation.

Two Zen Masters Establish a Clinic in South Shanghai 163

Benefiting the Poor and Sick

Zen Masters Xingci and Kai, abbots of the Fancang Temple on Rue Grosse in the French Concession, have profound knowledge of Buddhist scriptures and are particularly enthusiastic about local charitable undertakings. Recently, in view of the fact that there are many factories and residents in the South Shanghai area, but there are no suitable clinics for providing diagnosis and medicine nearby, which is very inconvenient for workers and the poor seeking treatment, they specially discussed with three lay Buddhists in Shanghai, Wang Yiting, Huang Hanzhi, and Guan Jiongzhi, to select a site at the intersection of Xieqiao Jumen Road and Yuwei Road to build a Fancang Temple clinic. The location is refreshing and the scale is grand. They also invited the famous Shanghai doctor Xia Yingtang to hire two doctors on their behalf. One is Ma Xin-hou, an expert in internal medicine and surgery, who is a descendant of the Menghe Ma Peizhi family. The other is Qin Liu-an, an expert in internal medicine, who is the younger brother of the famous local doctor Qin Bowei. Both Dr. Ma and Dr. Qin have profound family knowledge and rich experience, and the selection of doctors for this clinic can be said to be appropriate. Since the clinic opened on the 30th of last month, the number of people seeking diagnosis and treatment has been increasing day by day. On the first day, there were 45 patients, on the second day, there were 56 patients, and on the third day, there were 73 patients. The future development should not be inferior to the Renji Weizhong temples. As for the two Zen masters, they can be said to be the ones who remove all the suffering of all beings. It is also heard that the clinic plans to add a Western medicine room, and everything is currently being planned and will be realized soon.

Policeman Rapes and Occupies Another Man's Wife 164

＝The husband is unwilling but unable to resist＝

＝He hits the policeman's head with a stone by the roadside＝

Liu Dongming from Shandong, together with his concubine Ms. Xu, came to Shanghai from their hometown in early July of this year for sightseeing. They stayed in a workshop of a certain yarn factory on Yulin Road, and spent their days entertaining themselves in various amusement parks. Within two weeks, all the money they had brought was used up, and being unfamiliar with the place and people, they had nowhere to borrow. He remembered that he had relatives doing business in Qingdao, so on the 20th of that month, he went to Qingdao to borrow money. Ms. Xu remained in Shanghai. At that time, he said that he would return soon, but several months have passed without any news. Ms. Xu was naturally licentious and unaccustomed to sleeping alone, so she developed a physical relationship with Jiang Songmin, a fellow villager working as a Chinese policeman No. 2667. Their love was intense, and they lived together like a married couple, renting a house at No. 409 Qiwupu Road. Until 7 p.m. the day before yesterday, Liu Dongming returned to Shanghai from Qingdao by boat. When he returned home, the place was empty. He immediately found out that Ms. Xu and Jiang were living together. He rushed to negotiate. Ms. Xu admitted it without hesitation and gave him five Yuan silver coins, so Liu could return to Shandong and find another way to make a living. Liu was shocked and immediately became jealous, so he had a quarrel with Ms. Xu, parted in hatred, and wanted to find a way to deal with it. He wandered around Yangzhou Road. After a while, he saw Ms. Xu and Jiang going out together. He wanted to step forward and question them, but seeing Jiang the policeman's burly figure, he knew he could not defeat him. So, he picked up a piece of cement stone by the roadside, rushed up from behind, and hit Jiang's head hard. Jiang turned his head in pain, saw that it was Liu, and immediately wrestled him to the ground and beat him. Liu was no match for him after all. He jumped up and ran madly towards Qiwupu Road. Jiang the policeman did not give up and chased after him. The Indian policeman No. 109 on guard there saw Liu running towards him, and immediately stopped him. After questioning, he found out that it was a fight, so he took both parties to the police station. The police chief found out that both of them were injured, so he ordered them to be sent to the Chinese Patrol Hospital on Huade Road for treatment. After the doctor's examination, Liu Dongming's hand was injured, but there was no major problem. After applying medicine and bandaging, he was taken back to the police station. The next morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Wu Zehan interrogated him. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, stated the case, saying that Jiang the policeman was still in the hospital and had not recovered, so he should request a postponement. Then, according to Indian policeman No. 109 and the woman Jiang Xu, they testified about what happened. When asked, Liu Dongming confessed that Jiang the policeman should not have forcibly occupied another man's wife, and asked for a clear judgment. Judge Wu ordered him to be remanded in custody and the trial was postponed.

Chinese Warden Extorts Money from Prisoner's Family, Judged Guilty 165

Chen Yongnian from Pudong, the owner of Dexing Plank Box Shop at No. 92 Aidoa Road, was sentenced to imprisonment in the West Prison on Huade Road for theft. Around February of this year, Yu Jinshan, a Qingkou native who was Warden No. 39, falsely wrote letters under the pretext of the prisoner being ill, and went to Dexing Plank Box Shop to fraudulently collect seven silver dollars from his wife, Ms. Qin, for his own use. The case was discovered by the Chinese warden of the West Prison, who sent Warden Yu to the Huishan Police Station to be handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. This has been detailed in this newspaper. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiefen continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that Chen, the prisoner, and witness Wang San had been brought to court for cross-examination. Wang San then testified that he used to be Chinese policeman No. 84 in the West Prison and has now resigned. At that time, the defendant did give him the letter and asked him to collect 17 dollars from Chen's shop, promising to give him two dollars. Because he knew it was against the law, he was unwilling to go. Later, he went by himself, which is true. Chen Yongnian also testified that he did not write a letter to him. When asked, the defendant's confession was evasive. Judge Xiao verified the confession and announced the judgment in court, sentencing the defendant to six months' imprisonment and a fine of 100 dollars.

Worker Crushed to Death by Machine 166

Qiu Liangmin from Tongzhou, 21 years old, was a worker in the Lide Oil Factory at No. 78 Gordon Road. Yesterday morning around 8 o'clock, he was careless at work and was suddenly crushed in the head by an oil-pressing machine. He fell to the ground immediately and lost consciousness. Later, the factory reported to the Fire Brigade and sent an ambulance to take him to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, due to his serious injuries, the treatment was ineffective and he died around 1 p.m. His body was transferred to the morgue for examination.

Tobacco and Paper Store Robbed on Qiujiang Road 167

Tiancheng Tobacco and Paper Store at No. 217 Qiujiang Road, Zhabei, is owned by Liu Tianxi. It has been open for many years and the business is not bad, which has been coveted by bandits. Around 8 p.m. the night before last, two bandits wearing blue cloth and silk short shirts and trousers, each carrying a handgun and speaking with a Jiangbei accent, broke into the store and ordered the owner not to make any noise. They were robbed of 18 silver dollars and 150 cents in small silver coins. After the robbery, they carried the loot and fled. Afterwards, the owner reported to the Fifth District, First Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which immediately sent police to pursue and arrest them, but the robbers had already escaped without a trace.

Weather Report 177

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that the weather here is slightly cold, with occasional showers and gales, but it will gradually improve at night. The hurricane is approaching northeastward, heading towards southern Korea. There are cyclones and rain in the Korean Strait, and a great gale in the Yellow Sea. The center of the hurricane was about 60 miles within the intersection of 33 degrees north latitude and 125 degrees east longitude at 4:00 p.m., moving northeast with strong winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 83.7 and the lowest was 74.5. On the same day last year, the highest was 83.1 and the lowest was 66.2.

Special Article: The Revival of the Chinese Nation and the Women's Movement 178

— Wu Tiecheng

丨Speech at the Third National Congress of the National Women's Youth Association丨

Distinguished representatives, Shanghai feels very honored that your association has come to Shanghai to hold the Third National Congress. As the head of this city, I would like to express my warm welcome on behalf of the citizens. The representatives of this conference come from the rural areas of the Chinese mainland, and of course there are many from the cities. The statistical significance of this number of representatives is that it allows us to predict the success of this conference.

Distinguished representatives, coming to Shanghai from the mainland, you must recognize that Shanghai is an economic center of China; it is the location of a driving force for the whole of China. Shanghai has more than 3.1 million people, making it the fifth largest port in the world; it is not only the largest commercial port in China, but also one of the largest commercial ports in the Far East. Now Shanghai has already occupied an important position in the country in terms of economy, culture, and public opinion; but the increase in Shanghai's population is even more alarming. In Xianfeng five years, that is, more than 70 years ago, the Public Concession had only a few hundred people, and the whole city had only 30,000 to 40,000 people, but today there are more than 3.1 million. However, the reasons and conditions for the increase in Shanghai's population are different from those of cities in other countries around the world. The increase in the population of cities in other countries around the world is due to the convenience of transportation and the development of industry. However, the sudden increase in Shanghai's population is not due to the development of industry, but because of the continuous warfare in China for the past two or thirty years, social unrest, reduced production, unimproved production tools, and the imminent bankruptcy of the rural economy. The rich people have come to Shanghai, relying on the concessions to make a comfortable nest; the poor have also flocked to Shanghai to make a living. This has continued to increase Shanghai's population to 3.1 million. Therefore, the sudden increase in Shanghai's population is actually a symbol of the bankruptcy of our country's rural economy and the uneasy lives of our people. This is such a dangerous and terrible thing! Distinguished representatives, most of you come from the mainland, so when I welcome you today, I will briefly report the general situation of Shanghai to you. At the same time, I hope that you representatives will have time to conduct an on-the-spot investigation in Shanghai.

Distinguished representatives, you have come here from afar from the Chinese mainland. Although the Chinese mainland is not as prosperous as Shanghai, the people in the Chinese mainland are kind and the customs are good, which cannot be expected in the treaty ports. Therefore, representatives, when you see the prosperity and luxury of Shanghai, please do not envy it. You must know that China has reached the point of exhaustion. Under such circumstances, not only can our people not rise up to remedy the situation, work hard to improve production tools, increase production, and enrich national power; but the situation is getting worse and worse, and the leaks are increasing day by day. According to the Customs Report for the 20th year: Our trade deficit in China is 540 million; in other words, comparing the export and import of domestic and foreign goods every year, we still have to take 540 million out. If the national blood is leaked out like this for a long time, how can we not be poor! How can we not die! China has suffered from severe anemia, and the blood is gradually drying up; even without foreign troubles, without the military aggression and oppression of the Japanese, it can lead to death. This is indeed the most dangerous period in our country's history, so the only important task in China today is "national salvation," which the chairman just said. However, national salvation work should be jointly responsible by men and women. Although the national salvation work of men and the national salvation work of women may differ due to different positions; but their purpose is the same. The general theme set by this conference is "Building a New Society." This general theme really makes us express our heartfelt respect to the representatives; because our national salvation work varies among individuals due to different knowledge, abilities, opportunities, and environments. However, as long as all compatriots in the country, regardless of men or women, do their best with their intelligence, do a little, we will get a little achievement. This is truly beneficial to the country and beneficial to the people.

However, before we engage in national salvation work, we must also establish a goal; to revive our Chinese nation. The Chinese nation has thousands of years of history and has made great contributions to world civilization. Although modern European civilization is far better than our country, how can their civilization today not be inspired and influenced by the civilization of the Chinese nation thousands of years ago. The Chinese nation is the largest, most civilized, and most contributing nation in the world, but today it has fallen behind. The national spirit has also been so decadent. The reason for this is entirely because of the disappearance of our national self-confidence in the past few hundred years; because of the disappearance of national self-confidence, our Chinese people have not been able to promote the inherent creative ability of thousands of years. This is the biggest root cause of national decline. So, to save the country, we must first carry out the revival movement of the Chinese nation, and restore the self-confidence of the Chinese nation; if each of us takes the revival of the Chinese nation as the basic work of saving the country, and works hard with the spirit of bravely advancing, I believe that our country can definitely be saved. The general theme of this conference, "Building a New Society," is one of the most important and basic tasks in the revival movement of the Chinese nation. Every Chinese person has this great ambition, and I believe that the construction of a new society will definitely succeed. Our ancestors did a lot of great things thousands of years ago. Although we now have more opportunities for education and more opportunities for doing business than our ancestors, we are still far behind the things that our ancestors did. It is really a shame. Now the people of the whole country are calling for national salvation; however, national salvation is not just resisting Japan. Resisting Japan is a part of the work of saving the country. The work of saving the country is really a thousand and one things. We must contribute our bodies and all our strength to the society and to the country, and the work of saving the country cannot be completed. The work that women undertake is different from that of men, and women generally feel that their work of saving the country is not as direct and significant as that of men. In fact, I think women's responsibility is more important than that of men; especially the work of building a new society, women should take more responsibility, because the masters of the country in the future and the backbone of the new society in the future all depend on the education of women. The theme of this conference is "Building a New Society," which is deeply in line with the main points of the women's movement. I hope that the representatives will lead women all over the country to move towards this goal.

Finally, I also hope that when you go back to your hometowns, you will bring a message to the people in various places: To make Shanghai a truly prosperous city in name and reality, we must first revive the rural economy. The city is like a fish, and the inland rural area is like water. If the water dries up, the fish will have no way to survive. Now the rural economy in various places is bankrupt, like there is no water. The fish in the city can only die. Although Shanghai is so prosperous now, it is fake. To revive the Chinese nation and save the country, we must start from reviving the rural economy in various places, based on our inherent spirit and civilization of thousands of years, and accept modern Western civilization to build a new society and build a new China! Today I offer this idea to all the representatives and wish the representatives and the conference success.

Jiangsu Education Department Randomly Inspects Social Education Institutions in Various Counties 180

Sends Inspector Jin and Other Six People

To Re-examine Standard Work

The Jiangsu Education Department believes that the 21st year has ended, and the reports on the implementation of the minimum standard work of the public education centers and peasant education centers in various counties have been submitted to the department one after another. According to the eighth article of the Jiangsu Province's method of examining the implementation of the minimum standard work of the public education centers and peasant education centers in various counties, it is urgent to send personnel to various counties for random inspection to assess them. Inspector Jin Zonghua and other six people have been sent to various counties for random inspection, and they have set off one after another. The counties to be inspected by each person are listed below. Inspector Jin Zonghua will randomly inspect 11 counties including Jiangning, Jurong, Lishui, Gaochun, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jintan, Liyang, and Yangzhong. Inspector Cao Shutian will randomly inspect 8 counties including Wuxian, Changshu, Kunshan, Wujiang, Wuxi, Yixing, and Jiangyin. Inspector Shen Fu will randomly inspect 10 counties including Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, Qingpu, Fengxian, Jinshan, Chuansha, Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan. Compiler Peng Daquan will randomly inspect 7 counties including Nantong, Rugao, Chongming, Haimen, Jingjiang, Qidong, and Taixing. Compiler Sun Jiehuang will randomly inspect 12 counties including Tongshan, Fengxian, Peixian, Xiaoxian, Dangshan, Pixian, Suqian, Suining, Donghai, Guanyun, Shutang, and Ganyu. Section member Chen Wei will randomly inspect 13 counties including Huaiyin, Huaian, Siyang, Lianshui, Funing, Yancheng, Jiangdu, Yizheng, Dongtai, Xinghua, Taixian, Gaoyou, and Baoying.

Jiangsu Education Department Orders the Issuance of Teaching Progress Schedules for Each Subject in Senior and Junior High Schools 181

And Orders Compliance

The Jiangsu Education Department ordered that the academic level of each middle school in the province varies greatly, and the teaching progress also differs. The reason is that the teaching progress has not been determined, so that each subject cannot develop evenly. The Director of the Department, in view of this, has hired experts in each subject and several people with experience in secondary education to organize a committee to jointly study. For example, senior high school subjects such as civics, Chinese, English, mathematics, history, geography, physics, chemistry, biology, and ethics; and junior high school subjects such as civics, Chinese, English, mathematics, history, geography, botany, zoology, chemistry, and physics are assigned to be responsible for compiling the teaching progress schedules separately. Except for the civics subject, which should wait for the curriculum standards to be promulgated before compiling, the rest of the subjects are divided into detailed items and allocated to each week according to the outline listed in the senior and junior high school curriculum standards as the standard for implementation. It took several months and meetings to complete. The committee members based their teaching experience and carefully compiled the schedules. Although it is not perfect, it can also be used for practical teaching. Now that the school year has already begun, each middle school will open soon. The aforementioned progress schedules, except for the English subject, which is still being printed, have been printed. In addition to submitting them to the Ministry of Education for filing, they are also distributed. The aforementioned progress schedules are checked and issued, and a checklist is attached, ordering the director of each bureau to forward them to each middle school for compliance. From the new students of senior and junior high schools this year, they should be implemented uniformly. Each county's middle school's academic level is too different from the general standard, and they should earnestly follow this order to improve the level and unify the progress. They must not be insincere or ignore it. The Department will check the progress of each subject at any time based on each schedule to reward or punish them. It should still be reported first for record. As for the English progress schedule, it will be ordered and issued after it is printed. This order should be known.

浙敎廳 Orders All Counties and Cities to Improve Rural Public Schools

The Zhejiang Education Department believes that the rural economy is on the verge of collapse, and that the way to revitalize it lies not only in the economic aspect, but also in paying attention to the promotion and improvement of rural education. It has been found that in the past, the handling of public school education in various counties and cities of the province has often neglected rural areas, either by not establishing enough schools to accommodate the majority of the public, or by poor management leading to no results, or by stopping classes midway due to the busy farming season before the courses are completed. How can this achieve significant results? Educational administrative organs in all counties and cities must make efforts to correct this malpractice within this year. On the one hand, they should pay attention to improving the existing public schools in rural areas, and on the other hand, they should establish and open the planned public schools in rural areas before October this year, in order to complete the courses during the farming off-season from late autumn to early spring and hold graduation ceremonies.

Second Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Educational Film Association's Shanghai Branch 182

Concretely Stipulating the Implementation Plan of Various Undertakings

Educational Films to be Shown in Various Schools Starting October 1st

The Shanghai branch of the Chinese Educational Film Association, regarding the matter of showing educational films, has received instructions from the Municipal Education Bureau to cooperate with the private schools at all levels in the city to collect fees. Therefore, it convened the second joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on the afternoon of the other day to discuss the implementation plan. The attendees included committee members Pan Gongzhan, Tao Baichuan, Chen Bai, Zheng Zhengqiu, Yang Minshi, Lu Shibai, Zheng Hongnian, etc., chaired by Yang Minshi. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Report Items 183

Publication of "New Weapons, Volume 1" from the Shenbao Series 187

"New Weapons" is compiled and translated by Mr. Chen Changwei, based on the book "The Wonder of the Latest Weapons" published by the Japanese Shinkosha. With the increasingly developed science and technology, the killing, destructive, and annihilating capabilities of new weapons far exceed our imagination. The purpose of compiling and translating this book is to introduce the basic knowledge of new weapons to our people. Currently, the conflicts between the great powers are becoming increasingly blatant, and in the Second World War, China will inevitably be one of the main elements triggering the war. The preface states, "The god of war has descended upon the world. In order to strive for national survival and complete the historical mission, the fact has forced us to prepare, whether we are willing or unwilling. You will have to read this book." Its importance can be imagined. The whole book has twelve chapters, with forty-seven exquisite copper illustrations in the front. It is priced at forty cents and is published by the special distribution office of this newspaper. With the start of the autumn semester, a special price will be offered for one month. Purchases of ten or more copies will be calculated at a 30% discount.

New Experiment at Jiangqiao Primary School in Shanghai County's Free Education Experimental Zone 192

Director Shi of the Shanghai County Education Bureau, in view of the large number of unemployed people near the county seat, which urgently needs to be remedied, has specially designated the southeast three miles of the new county seat as a free education experimental zone. Jiangqiao Primary School is one of the schools in the experimental zone. The school is located in Jiangqiao Township, southeast of the Shanghai County Government. In order to implement free education, the school does not charge tuition fees. All school-age children in the school district must be forced to enroll. In order to adapt to the countryside and facilitate children to help with farm work, a short-term system is adopted. The curriculum is divided into four types: reading, composition, writing, and arithmetic. All students who have completed 540 hours of instruction have completed the short-term free education. There are currently 80 students, divided into morning and afternoon classes. It is heard that the principal is Ni Zhimin, a graduate of the first class of Shanghai County Rural Model [school]. Mr. Ni is simple and honest, happy to live in the countryside, and is quite trusted by farmers.

丨 Already Working at Shanghai Qinfen Bookstore

Mr. Fu Baolu from Harbin is a nationally renowned creator of China's highest pole vault record, with a score of 3.54 meters. Recently, he created an unofficial record of 3.80 meters, which is amazing. It is found that Mr. Fu is only 20 years old, a handsome young man, and works in the Harbin Railway. However, since the fall of the Northeast, he has been closely monitored by the puppet organization and is unwilling to be oppressed by others. He escaped from the tiger's mouth, arrived in Shanghai via Dalian, and sought a decent job so that he could practice with peace of mind in his spare time. Qingguang Defeats Xiaguang in Last Night's Basketball Game 198

Result: 55 to 23

丨 Qingguang vs. Tongji Tonight at 7:30丨

The Qingguang Basketball Team from Nanjing made its debut last night against the Xiaguang Team from Daxia University at the China Basketball Gym. Wei Haiqing, Xian Zhuanghuai, Zhou Jun, etc. of Qingguang have long been famous and performed quite well. The Xiaguang team has uneven talent, and its offense and defense are inferior. As a result, Qingguang won by 55 to 23. In the first half, Qingguang scored 23 points and Xiaguang scored 14 points. Tonight at 7:30, Qingguang will play against the Youth Association at the China Basketball Gym.

After the start of the game, after several back-and-forths, Wei Haiqing, the center of Qingguang, scored two consecutive goals. Chen Baoqiu of Xiaguang selected one. At that time, both sides seemed to be in the initial test period, and the situation was not yet tense. Qingguang had many opportunities to throw the ball, but there were few long shots that hit the target, and all relied on close shots to score points. The rear defense was tight, and Xiaguang was weak and had no opportunity to make a plan. Qingguang once took the lead by 14 to 2. Xiaguang started to add two points by Ren [blank] Xing. Afterwards, Qingguang's momentum gradually increased, and Xian Zhuanghuai and Guo Zhen frequently scored, taking a remote lead by 22 to 4. Xiaguang reinvigorated and gradually expanded, and [blank] An and Ren Jiexing added ten points in a row, creating 14 to 22 at the end of the first half.

From the beginning of the second half, Xiaguang's momentum suddenly increased, and the competition became fierce. The scores increased each other, but after five minutes of stalemate, Xiaguang felt unable to support it, while Qingguang was in its heyday and its momentum was like a flame. Therefore, the situation became one-sided from then on. When Xiaguang scored 19 points, Qingguang had already scored 45 points. Xiaguang's lineup was chaotic and deteriorated. In the final result, Qingguang won by 55 to 23. Referee Zhou Jiaqi, the scores are as follows:
